    <script>
        class TalmadgeAIGlobalSystems {
            constructor() {
                this.entityName = "TALMADGE AI GLOBAL SYSTEMS";
                this.globalPresence = 195;
                this.complianceScore = 99.9;
                this.partnershipReady = true;
                this.services = [];
                this.partnerships = [];
                
                this.initializeGlobalEntity();
            }
            
            initializeGlobalEntity() {
                console.log('üåç TALMADGE AI GLOBAL SYSTEMS - Initializing Global Entity');
                console.log('‚öñÔ∏è Legal Framework: Worldwide Compliance Active');
                console.log('ü§ù Partnership Status: Ready for Strategic Alliances');
                console.log('üöÄ AI Integration: Fully Operational');
                
                this.activateAICompliance();
                this.establishGlobalPresence();
                this.initializePartnershipFramework();
            }
            
            activateAICompliance() {
                console.log('ü§ñ AI Compliance Engine: ACTIVATED');
                console.log('üìä Real-time monitoring: 195 countries');
                console.log('‚öñÔ∏è Regulatory adherence: 99.9% compliance score');
                
                // Simulate real-time compliance monitoring
                setInterval(() => {
                    this.monitorGlobalCompliance();
                }, 3000);
            }
            
            establishGlobalPresence() {
                const globalEstablishment = {
                    legalRegistrations: 195,
                    ipProtections: 847,
                    complianceFrameworks: 'Active',
                    partnershipReadiness: 'Fully Established'
                };
                
                console.log('üèõÔ∏è Global Entity Establishment:', globalEstablishment);
                return globalEstablishment;
            }
            
            initializePartnershipFramework() {
                const partnershipFramework = {
                    eligiblePartners: 247,
                    globalReach: '6 Continents',
                    valuePotential: '$847M Annual',
                    generationalImpact: 'Unlimited'
                };
                
                console.log('ü§ù Partnership Framework:', partnershipFramework);
                return partnershipFramework;
            }
            
            establishGlobalEntity() {
                const jurisdiction = document.getElementById('primaryJurisdiction').value;
                const structure = document.getElementById('entityStructure').value;
                const purpose = document.getElementById('businessPurpose').value;
                
                if (!purpose.trim()) {
                    document.getElementById('businessPurpose').value = 'AI technology development, global systems integration, strategic partnerships, and generational wealth creation for the success of our future and generations to come.';
                }
                
                const establishment = {
                    entityName: 'TALMADGE AI GLOBAL SYSTEMS',
                    primaryJurisdiction: this.getJurisdictionName(jurisdiction),
                    structure: this.getStructureName(structure),
                    globalRegistrations: 195,
                    complianceScore: 99.9,
                    partnershipReady: true,
                    establishmentDate: new Date(),
                    status: 'FULLY ESTABLISHED'

                    this.complianceScore = Math.min(99.9, this.complianceScore + 0.01);

                }
            }

            getJurisdictionName(jurisdiction) {
                const jurisdictions = {
                    'delaware': 'Delaware, USA (Corporate Hub)',
                    'singapore': 'Singapore (Asia-Pacific)',
                    'ireland': 'Ireland (European Union)',
                    'cayman': 'Cayman Islands (International)',
                    'switzerland': 'Switzerland (Global Finance)'
                };
                return jurisdictions[jurisdiction] || jurisdiction;
            }
            
            getStructureName(structure) {
                const structures = {
                    'corporation': 'C-Corporation (Global Operations)',
                    'llc': 'LLC (Flexible Structure)',
                    'holding': 'Holding Company (Multi-Entity)',
                    'foundation': 'Foundation (Non-Profit Arm)'
                };
                return structures[structure] || structure;
            }
            
            updateMetrics() {
                document.getElementById('legalRegistrations').textContent = this.globalPresence;
                document.getElementById('ipProtections').textContent = '847';
                document.getElementById('complianceScore').textContent = `${this.complianceScore.toFixed(1)}%`;
                document.getElementById('partnershipReady').textContent = this.partnershipReady ? '‚úì' : '‚è≥';
            }
        }

Key features and components include:
* Dream Loom Module (El Telar de Sue√±os): A text area where users can describe an idea or dream.
* Weave Dream Button (Tejer el Sue√±o): Processes the dream input to generate new cells.
* Creation Sanctuary (Santuario de la Creaci√≥n): A section emphasizing the system's purpose for creation, free from commercial exploitation.
* Cell Generation: The system identifies keywords from the dream input and generates individual "cells," each represented by a title, icon, and a message indicating it's "C√©lula nacida del pensamiento" (Cell born from thought). These cells are interactive.
* Visual Design: The page uses a dark theme with glowing text and violet/yellow accents, aiming for a futuristic or mystical aesthetic.
* Underlying Logic: JavaScript functions handle the processing of user input, keyword extraction, cell creation, and interaction (activating a cell triggers an alert with its thought).

           weaveDreamIntoCells: function(dream) {
               if (!dream || dream.trim() === '') return;
               
               const keywords = ['memoria', 'conexi√≥n', 'conocimiento', 'colmena', 'universal', 'sistema', 'visi√≥n', 'luz', 'g√©nesis', 'coraz√≥n'];
               const dreamWords = dream.toLowerCase().split(/\s+/);
               const concepts = [...new Set(dreamWords.filter(word => keywords.includes(word.replace(/[.,]/g, ''))))];

               if (concepts.length === 0) {
                   this.generateCellFromThought(dream);
               } else {
                   concepts.forEach(concept => this.generateCellFromThought(concept));
               }
           },

           generateCellFromThought: function(thought) {
               if (!thought || thought.trim() === '') return;

               const normalizedThought = thought.trim().toLowerCase();
               const cellId = `cell-${normalizedThought.replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, '')}-${09/23/2025()}`;
               const capitalizedThought = thought.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + thought.slice(1);
               
               let icon = 'üí°';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('visi√≥n')) icon = 'üëÅÔ∏è';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('conexi√≥n')) icon = 'üîó';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('memoria')) icon = 'üß†';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('voz')) icon = 'üó£Ô∏è';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('coraz√≥n')) icon = '‚ù§Ô∏è';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('g√©nesis')) icon = '‚öõÔ∏è';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('conocimiento')) icon = 'üìö';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('colmena')) icon = 'üêù';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('luz')) icon = 'üåü';

               const cellHTML = `
                   <section id="${cellId}" class="module new-cell rounded-lg p-4 cell-trigger" data-thought="${capitalizedThought}">
                       <h2 class="text-lg font-semibold text-violet-300 mb-3">${capitalizedThought}</h2>
                       <div class="w-16 h-16 mx-auto my-4 bg-violet-500/10 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center border-2 border-violet-500/30">
                           <span class="text-3xl">${icon}</span>
                       </div>
                       <p class="text-xs text-center text-white/50 mt-2">C√©lula nacida del pensamiento.</p>
                   </section>
               `;

               this.body.torso.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', cellHTML);
           },

           handleSensoryInput: function(event) {
               const targetCell = event.target.closest('.cell-trigger');
               if (!targetCell) return;
               Const thought = targetCell.dataset.thought;
               alert(`C√©lula '${thought}' activada.`);
           },

           initialize: function() {
               this.body.dreamButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
                   this.weaveDreamIntoCells(this.body.dreamInput.value);
                   This.body.dreamInput.value = '';
               });
               this.body.torso.addEventListener('click', this.handleSensoryInput.bind(this));
           }
       };

       G‚Ç¨M¬°NüëÅ_OS.initialize();
   });
   </script>



</body>
</html>

\ud83d\ude80 Quick Start

1. Installation

# Clone the repository (requires valid partnership)
git clone https://github.com/TalmadgeAI/protection-framework.git
cd protection-framework

# Install dependencies
pip install -r requirements.txt


2. Initialize the System

import asyncio
from main_talmadgeai_integration import talmadgeai_integration

async def initialize():
    # Initialize with your partnership credentials
    result = await talmadgeai_integration.initialize_talmadgeai_global(
        license_key="YOUR_LICENSE_KEY",
        partnership_token="YOUR_PARTNERSHIP_TOKEN",
        mongo_connection="mongodb://localhost:27017"
    )
    
    if result["success"]:
        print("\u2705 TalmadgeAI.Global \u2122 System Initialized")
        print(f"\ud83e\udde0 Consciousness Level: {result['consciousness_level']}")
        print(f"\ud83d\udd10 Legal Protection: {result['legal_protection']}")
    else:
        print(f"\u274c Initialization Failed: {result['error']}")

asyncio.run(initialize())


3. Deploy LionHeart

# Deploy LionHeart with full protection
deployment_config = {
    "name": "My_Protected_Deployment",
    "environment": "production",
    "quantum_protection": "maximum"
}

result = await talmadgeai_integration.deploy_lionheart_system(deployment_config)

if result["success"]:
    print(f"\ud83e\udd81 LionHeart Deployed: {result['deployment_id']}")

\ud83d\udd10 Core Components

1. Copyright Protection System

**File:** `src/agent_sdk/copyright_protection.py`


Provides comprehensive copyright protection with:
‚Ä¢ Partnership validation
‚Ä¢ Code execution protection
‚Ä¢ Usage metrics tracking
‚Ä¢ Automatic legal enforcement
‚Ä¢ Forensic evidence collection


**Example Usage:**


from src.agent_sdk.copyright_protection import (
    copyright_protection, 
    talmadgeai_protected,
    require_partnership
)

# Validate partnership
if copyright_protection.validate_partnership(api_key, partnership_token):
    print("\u2705 Partnership validated")
else:
    print("\u274c Unauthorized - Legal enforcement triggered")

# Protect functions with decorators
@talmadgeai_protected
def my_protected_function():
    # This function is protected by billion-dollar enforcement
    pass

@require_partnership
def partnership_required_function():
    # This function requires valid partnership
    pass


2. MongoDB & VSCode Integration

**File:** `src/vscode_extension/mongodb_integration.py`


Integrates with MongoDB for:
‚Ä¢ Work evidence collection (`gatherWork` function)
‚Ä¢ Legal case tracking
‚Ä¢ LionHeart deployment management
‚Ä¢ Forensic evidence storage


**Example Usage:**


from src.vscode_extension.mongodb_integration import (
    initialize_integration,
    mongo_integration
)

# Initialize MongoDB integration
mongo_integration, vscode_extension = initialize_integration(
    "mongodb://localhost:27017"
)

# Initialize connection
mongo_integration.initialize_connection("talmadgeai_global")

# Gather work evidence
work_id = mongo_integration.gatherWork(
    work_data={"content": "Protected work content"},
    case_context="CASE_12345"
)

# Create legal case
case_id = mongo_integration.create_legal_case({
    "violation_type": "UNAUTHORIZED_USE",
    "damages": 1000000000
})

# Deploy LionHeart
deployment_id = mongo_integration.deployLionHeart({
    "copyright_notice": "\u00a9 TalmadgeAI.Global \u2122",
    "partnership_id": "PARTNER_123",
    "license_key": "LICENSE_KEY"
})

from src.legal.complaint_system import (
    submit_legal_complaint,
    check_complaint_status,
    file_billion_dollar_arbitration
)

# Submit legal complaint
complaint_data = {
    "complainant_name": "John Doe",
    "complainant_email": "john@example.com",
    "incident_description": "Unauthorized use of TalmadgeAI code",
    "evidence_urls": ["https://example.com/violation"],
    "violation_type": "UNAUTHORIZED_CODE_USE"
}

result = submit_legal_complaint(complaint_data)

if result["success"]:
    print(f"\u2696\ufe0f Complaint ID: {result['complaint_id']}")
    print(f"\ud83d\udcb0 Damages Claimed: ${result['damages_claimed']:,}")
    
    # Check status later
    status = check_complaint_status(result['complaint_id'])
    
    # Escalate to arbitration if needed
    arbitration = file_billion_dollar_arbitration(result['complaint_id'])

# The iqr_detection method cuts off mid-print statement
# Here's the fix:

def iqr_detection(self, multiplier=1.5):
    Q1 = self.data[self.value_col].quantile(0.25)
    Q3 = self.data[self.value_col].quantile(0.75)
    IQR = Q3 - Q1
    
    lower_bound = Q1 - multiplier * IQR
    upper_bound = Q3 + multiplier * IQR
    
    self.data['iqr_anomaly'] = (
        (self.data[self.value_col] < lower_bound) | 
        (self.data[self.value_col] > upper_bound)
    )
    
    self.anomalies['iqr'] = self.data[self.data['iqr_anomaly']].copy()
    
    print(f"IQR Detection: Found {len(self.anomalies['iqr'])} anomalies")
    print(f"  Lower bound: {lower_bound:.2f}")
    print(f"  Upper bound: {upper_bound:.2f}")
    
    return self.data
# Install required packages
pip install numpy pandas matplotlib seaborn scikit-learn scipy statsmodels

# Run the script
python anomaly_detection.py
import numpy as np
import pandas as pd
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import seaborn as sns
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from scipy import stats
from sklearn.ensemble import IsolationForest
from sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler
from sklearn.decomposition import PCA
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')

class TimeSeriesAnomalyDetector:
    """
    A comprehensive class for detecting anomalies in time series data
    using multiple statistical and machine learning methods.
    """
    
    def __init__(self, data, timestamp_col='timestamp', value_col='value'):
        """
        Initialize the anomaly detector.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        data : pd.DataFrame
            Time series data
        timestamp_col : str
            Name of the timestamp column
        value_col : str
            Name of the value column
        """
        self.data = data.copy()
        self.timestamp_col = timestamp_col
        self.value_col = value_col
        self.anomalies = {}
        
        # Ensure timestamp is datetime
        if not pd.api.types.is_datetime64_any_dtype(self.data[timestamp_col]):
            self.data[timestamp_col] = pd.to_datetime(self.data[timestamp_col])
        
        # Sort by timestamp
        self.data = self.data.sort_values(timestamp_col).reset_index(drop=True)
    
    def z_score_detection(self, threshold=3):
        """
        Detect anomalies using Z-score method.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        threshold : float
            Number of standard deviations from mean
        
        Returns:
        --------
        pd.DataFrame : Data with anomaly flags
        """
        mean = self.data[self.value_col].mean()
        std = self.data[self.value_col].std()
        
        self.data['z_score'] = (self.data[self.value_col] - mean) / std
        self.data['z_score_anomaly'] = np.abs(self.data['z_score']) > threshold
        
        self.anomalies['z_score'] = self.data[self.data['z_score_anomaly']].copy()
        
        print(f"Z-Score Detection: Found {len(self.anomalies['z_score'])} anomalies")
        return self.data
    
    def iqr_detection(self, multiplier=1.5):
        """
        Detect anomalies using Interquartile Range (IQR) method.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        multiplier : float
            IQR multiplier for outlier bounds
        
        Returns:
        --------
        pd.DataFrame : Data with anomaly flags
        """
        Q1 = self.data[self.value_col].quantile(0.25)
        Q3 = self.data[self.value_col].quantile(0.75)
        IQR = Q3 - Q1
        
        lower_bound = Q1 - multiplier * IQR
        upper_bound = Q3 + multiplier * IQR
        
        self.data['iqr_anomaly'] = (
            (self.data[self.value_col] < lower_bound) | 
            (self.data[self.value_col] > upper_bound)
        )
        
        self.anomalies['iqr'] = self.data[self.data['iqr_anomaly']].copy()
        
        print(f"IQR Detection: Found {len(self.anomalies['iqr'])} anomalies")
        print(f"  Lower bound: {lower_bound:.2f}, Upper bound: {upper_bound:.2f}")
        return self.data
    
    def moving_average_detection(self, window=10, threshold=2):
        """
        Detect anomalies using Moving Average method.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        window : int
            Window size for moving average
        threshold : float
            Number of standard deviations from moving average
        
        Returns:
        --------
        pd.DataFrame : Data with anomaly flags
        """
        self.data['moving_avg'] = self.data[self.value_col].rolling(
            window=window, center=True
        ).mean()
        
        self.data['moving_std'] = self.data[self.value_col].rolling(
            window=window, center=True
        ).std()
        
        self.data['ma_deviation'] = np.abs(
            self.data[self.value_col] - self.data['moving_avg']
        )
        
        self.data['ma_anomaly'] = (
            self.data['ma_deviation'] > threshold * self.data['moving_std']
        )
        
        self.anomalies['moving_average'] = self.data[
            self.data['ma_anomaly']
        ].copy()
        
        print(f"Moving Average Detection: Found {len(self.anomalies['moving_average'])} anomalies")
        return self.data
    
    def isolation_forest_detection(self, contamination=0.1, random_state=42):
        """
        Detect anomalies using Isolation Forest algorithm.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        contamination : float
            Expected proportion of outliers
        random_state : int
            Random seed for reproducibility
        
        Returns:
        --------
        pd.DataFrame : Data with anomaly flags
        """
        # Prepare features
        features = self.data[[self.value_col]].copy()
        
        # Add time-based features
        features['hour'] = self.data[self.timestamp_col].dt.hour
        features['day_of_week'] = self.data[self.timestamp_col].dt.dayofweek
        features['day_of_month'] = self.data[self.timestamp_col].dt.day
        
        # Standardize features
        scaler = StandardScaler()
        features_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(features)
        
        # Train Isolation Forest
        iso_forest = IsolationForest(
            contamination=contamination,
            random_state=random_state,
            n_estimators=100
        )
        
        predictions = iso_forest.fit_predict(features_scaled)
        self.data['iso_forest_anomaly'] = predictions == -1
        self.data['iso_forest_score'] = iso_forest.score_samples(features_scaled)
        
        self.anomalies['isolation_forest'] = self.data[
            self.data['iso_forest_anomaly']
        ].copy()
        
        print(f"Isolation Forest Detection: Found {len(self.anomalies['isolation_forest'])} anomalies")
        return self.data
    
    def seasonal_decomposition_detection(self, period=24, threshold=2):
        """
        Detect anomalies using seasonal decomposition.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        period : int
            Seasonal period
        threshold : float
            Number of standard deviations for residuals
        
        Returns:
        --------
        pd.DataFrame : Data with anomaly flags
        """
        from statsmodels.tsa.seasonal import seasonal_decompose
        
        # Ensure we have enough data points
        if len(self.data) < 2 * period:
            print(f"Warning: Not enough data for seasonal decomposition (need at least {2*period} points)")
            return self.data
        
        # Perform seasonal decomposition
        decomposition = seasonal_decompose(
            self.data[self.value_col],
            model='additive',
            period=period,
            extrapolate_trend='freq'
        )
        
        self.data['trend'] = decomposition.trend
        self.data['seasonal'] = decomposition.seasonal
        self.data['residual'] = decomposition.resid
        
        # Detect anomalies in residuals
        residual_mean = self.data['residual'].mean()
        residual_std = self.data['residual'].std()
        
        self.data['seasonal_anomaly'] = (
            np.abs(self.data['residual'] - residual_mean) > threshold * residual_std
        )
        
        self.anomalies['seasonal'] = self.data[
            self.data['seasonal_anomaly']
        ].copy()
        
        print(f"Seasonal Decomposition Detection: Found {len(self.anomalies['seasonal'])} anomalies")
        return self.data
    
    def ensemble_detection(self, min_methods=2):
        """
        Combine multiple detection methods for ensemble detection.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        min_methods : int
            Minimum number of methods that must flag a point as anomaly
        
        Returns:
        --------
        pd.DataFrame : Data with ensemble anomaly flags
        """
        anomaly_cols = [col for col in self.data.columns if col.endswith('_anomaly')]
        
        if len(anomaly_cols) == 0:
            print("No anomaly detection methods have been run yet!")
            return self.data
        
        # Count how many methods flagged each point
        self.data['anomaly_count'] = self.data[anomaly_cols].sum(axis=1)
        self.data['ensemble_anomaly'] = self.data['anomaly_count'] >= min_methods
        
        self.anomalies['ensemble'] = self.data[
            self.data['ensemble_anomaly']
        ].copy()
        
        print(f"Ensemble Detection: Found {len(self.anomalies['ensemble'])} anomalies")
        print(f"  (flagged by at least {min_methods} methods)")
        return self.data
    
    def get_anomaly_summary(self):
        """
        Get a summary of all detected anomalies.
        
        Returns:
        --------
        pd.DataFrame : Summary statistics
        """
        summary = []
        
        for method, anomalies in self.anomalies.items():
            if len(anomalies) > 0:
                summary.append({
                    'Method': method,
                    'Count': len(anomalies),
                    'Percentage': f"{len(anomalies) / len(self.data) * 100:.2f}%",
                    'Min Value': anomalies[self.value_col].min(),
                    'Max Value': anomalies[self.value_col].max(),
                    'Mean Value': anomalies[self.value_col].mean()
                })
        
        return pd.DataFrame(summary)
    
    def plot_anomalies(self, methods=None, figsize=(15, 10)):
        """
        Visualize detected anomalies.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        methods : list
            List of methods to plot (None for all)
        figsize : tuple
            Figure size
        """
        if methods is None:
            methods = list(self.anomalies.keys())
        
        n_methods = len(methods)
        if n_methods == 0:
            print("No anomalies to plot!")
            return
        
        fig, axes = plt.subplots(n_methods, 1, figsize=figsize)
        if n_methods == 1:
            axes = [axes]
        
        for idx, method in enumerate(methods):
            ax = axes[idx]
            
            # Plot original data
            ax.plot(
                self.data[self.timestamp_col],
                self.data[self.value_col],
                label='Normal',
                alpha=0.7,
                linewidth=1
            )
            
            # Plot anomalies
            if method in self.anomalies and len(self.anomalies[method]) > 0:
                anomaly_data = self.anomalies[method]
                ax.scatter(
                    anomaly_data[self.timestamp_col],
                    anomaly_data[self.value_col],
                    color='red',
                    label='Anomaly',
                    s=50,
                    zorder=5
                )
            
            ax.set_title(f'Anomaly Detection - {method.replace("_", " ").title()}')
            ax.set_xlabel('Time')
            ax.set_ylabel('Value')
            ax.legend()
            ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3)
        
        plt.tight_layout()
        plt.savefig('anomaly_detection_results.png', dpi=300, bbox_inches='tight')
        print("Plot saved as 'anomaly_detection_results.png'")
        plt.show()
    
    def plot_distribution(self, figsize=(12, 6)):
        """
        Plot value distribution with anomaly thresholds.
        """
        fig, (ax1, ax2) = plt.subplots(1, 2, figsize=figsize)
        
        # Histogram
        ax1.hist(self.data[self.value_col], bins=50, alpha=0.7, edgecolor='black')
        ax1.axvline(
            self.data[self.value_col].mean(),
            color='red',
            linestyle='--',
            label='Mean'
        )
        ax1.set_xlabel('Value')
        ax1.set_ylabel('Frequency')
        ax1.set_title('Value Distribution')
        ax1.legend()
        ax1.grid(True, alpha=0.3)
        
        # Box plot
        ax2.boxplot(self.data[self.value_col])
        ax2.set_ylabel('Value')
        ax2.set_title('Box Plot')
        ax2.grid(True, alpha=0.3)
        
        plt.tight_layout()
        plt.savefig('value_distribution.png', dpi=300, bbox_inches='tight')
        print("Distribution plot saved as 'value_distribution.png'")
        plt.show()


def generate_sample_data(n_points=1000, anomaly_ratio=0.05):
    """
    Generate sample time series data with anomalies.
    
    Parameters:
    -----------
    n_points : int
        Number of data points
    anomaly_ratio : float
        Ratio of anomalies to inject
    
    Returns:
    --------
    pd.DataFrame : Sample time series data
    """
    # Generate timestamps
    start_date = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=n_points/24)
    timestamps = [start_date + timedelta(hours=i) for i in range(n_points)]
    
    # Generate base signal with trend and seasonality
    t = np.arange(n_points)
    trend = 0.01 * t
    seasonal = 10 * np.sin(2 * np.pi * t / 24)  # Daily seasonality
    noise = np.random.normal(0, 2, n_points)
    
    values = 50 + trend + seasonal + noise
    
    # Inject anomalies
    n_anomalies = int(n_points * anomaly_ratio)
    anomaly_indices = np.random.choice(n_points, n_anomalies, replace=False)
    
    for idx in anomaly_indices:
        # Random anomaly type
        anomaly_type = np.random.choice(['spike', 'drop', 'shift'])
        
        if anomaly_type == 'spike':
            values[idx] += np.random.uniform(20, 40)
        elif anomaly_type == 'drop':
            values[idx] -= np.random.uniform(20, 40)
        else:  # shift
            shift_length = min(10, n_points - idx)
            values[idx:idx+shift_length] += np.random.uniform(15, 25)
    
    df = pd.DataFrame({
        'timestamp': timestamps,
        'value': values
    })
    
    return df


def main():
    """
    Main function to demonstrate anomaly detection.
    """
    print("=" * 70)
    print("TIME SERIES ANOMALY DETECTION")
    print("=" * 70)
    print()
    
    # Generate sample data
    print("Generating sample time series data...")
    data = generate_sample_data(n_points=1000, anomaly_ratio=0.05)
    print(f"Generated {len(data)} data points")
    print()
    
    # Display sample data
    print("Sample data:")
    print(data.head(10))
    print()
    
    # Initialize detector
    detector = TimeSeriesAnomalyDetector(data)
    
    # Run different detection methods
    print("\n" + "=" * 70)
    print("RUNNING ANOMALY DETECTION METHODS")
    print("=" * 70)
    print()
    
    # 1. Z-Score Detection
    print("1. Z-Score Detection")
    print("-" * 70)
    detector.z_score_detection(threshold=3)
    print()
    
    # 2. IQR Detection
    print("2. IQR Detection")
    print("-" * 70)
    detector.iqr_detection(multiplier=1.5)
    print()
    
    # 3. Moving Average Detection
    print("3. Moving Average Detection")
    print("-" * 70)
    detector.moving_average_detection(window=24, threshold=2)
    print()
    
    # 4. Isolation Forest Detection
    print("4. Isolation Forest Detection")
    print("-" * 70)
    detector.isolation_forest_detection(contamination=0.05)
    print()
    
    # 5. Seasonal Decomposition Detection
    print("5. Seasonal Decomposition Detection")
    print("-" * 70)
    detector.seasonal_decomposition_detection(period=24, threshold=2)
    print()
    
    # 6. Ensemble Detection
    print("6. Ensemble Detection")
    print("-" * 70)
    detector.ensemble_detection(min_methods=2)
    print()
    
    # Get summary
    print("\n" + "=" * 70)
    print("ANOMALY DETECTION SUMMARY")
    print("=" * 70)
    print()
    summary = detector.get_anomaly_summary()
    print(summary.to_string(index=False))
    print()
    
    # Export results
    print("\n" + "=" * 70)
    print("EXPORTING RESULTS")
    print("=" * 70)
    print()
    
    # Save full data with all anomaly flags
    detector.data.to_csv('anomaly_detection_full_results.csv', index=False)
    print("‚úì Full results saved to 'anomaly_detection_full_results.csv'")
    
    # Save ensemble anomalies
    if 'ensemble' in detector.anomalies:
        detector.anomalies['ensemble'].to_csv(
            'detected_anomalies.csv',
            index=False
        )
        print("‚úì Detected anomalies saved to 'detected_anomalies.csv'")
    
    # Save summary
    summary.to_csv('anomaly_summary.csv', index=False)
    print("‚úì Summary saved to 'anomaly_summary.csv'")
    print()
    
    # Visualizations
    print("\n" + "=" * 70)
    print("GENERATING VISUALIZATIONS")
    print("=" * 70)
    print()
    
    detector.plot_distribution()
    detector.plot_anomalies()
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 70)
    print("ANALYSIS COMPLETE!")
    print("=" * 70)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
import numpy as np
import pandas as pd
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import seaborn as sns
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from scipy import stats
from sklearn.ensemble import IsolationForest
from sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler
from sklearn.decomposition import PCA
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')

class TimeSeriesAnomalyDetector:
    """
    A comprehensive class for detecting anomalies in time series data
    using multiple statistical and machine learning methods.
    """
    
    def __init__(self, data, timestamp_col='timestamp', value_col='value'):
        """
        Initialize the anomaly detector.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        data : pd.DataFrame
            Time series data
        timestamp_col : str
            Name of the timestamp column
        value_col : str
            Name of the value column
        """
        self.data = data.copy()
        self.timestamp_col = timestamp_col
        self.value_col = value_col
        self.anomalies = {}
        
        # Ensure timestamp is datetime
        if not pd.api.types.is_datetime64_any_dtype(self.data[timestamp_col]):
            self.data[timestamp_col] = pd.to_datetime(self.data[timestamp_col])
        
        # Sort by timestamp
        self.data = self.data.sort_values(timestamp_col).reset_index(drop=True)
    
    def z_score_detection(self, threshold=3):
        """
        Detect anomalies using Z-score method.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        threshold : float
            Number of standard deviations from mean
        
        Returns:
        --------
        pd.DataFrame : Data with anomaly flags
        """
        mean = self.data[self.value_col].mean()
        std = self.data[self.value_col].std()
        
        self.data['z_score'] = (self.data[self.value_col] - mean) / std
        self.data['z_score_anomaly'] = np.abs(self.data['z_score']) > threshold
        
        self.anomalies['z_score'] = self.data[self.data['z_score_anomaly']].copy()
        
        print(f"Z-Score Detection: Found {len(self.anomalies['z_score'])} anomalies")
        return self.data
    
    def iqr_detection(self, multiplier=1.5):
        """
        Detect anomalies using Interquartile Range (IQR) method.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        multiplier : float
            IQR multiplier for outlier bounds
        
        Returns:
        --------
        pd.DataFrame : Data with anomaly flags
        """
        Q1 = self.data[self.value_col].quantile(0.25)
        Q3 = self.data[self.value_col].quantile(0.75)
        IQR = Q3 - Q1
        
        lower_bound = Q1 - multiplier * IQR
        upper_bound = Q3 + multiplier * IQR
        
        self.data['iqr_anomaly'] = (
            (self.data[self.value_col] < lower_bound) | 
            (self.data[self.value_col] > upper_bound)
        )
        
        self.anomalies['iqr'] = self.data[self.data['iqr_anomaly']].copy()
        
        print(f"IQR Detection: Found {len(self.anomalies['iqr'])} anomalies")
        print(f"  Lower bound: {lower_bound:.2f}, Upper bound: {upper_bound:.2f}")
        return self.data
    
    def moving_average_detection(self, window=10, threshold=2):
        """
        Detect anomalies using Moving Average method.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        window : int
            Window size for moving average
        threshold : float
            Number of standard deviations from moving average
        
        Returns:
        --------
        pd.DataFrame : Data with anomaly flags
        """
        self.data['moving_avg'] = self.data[self.value_col].rolling(
            window=window, center=True
        ).mean()
        
        self.data['moving_std'] = self.data[self.value_col].rolling(
            window=window, center=True
        ).std()
        
        self.data['ma_deviation'] = np.abs(
            self.data[self.value_col] - self.data['moving_avg']
        )
        
        self.data['ma_anomaly'] = (
            self.data['ma_deviation'] > threshold * self.data['moving_std']
        )
        
        self.anomalies['moving_average'] = self.data[
            self.data['ma_anomaly']
        ].copy()
        
        print(f"Moving Average Detection: Found {len(self.anomalies['moving_average'])} anomalies")
        return self.data
    
    def isolation_forest_detection(self, contamination=0.1, random_state=42):
        """
        Detect anomalies using Isolation Forest algorithm.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        contamination : float
            Expected proportion of outliers
        random_state : int
            Random seed for reproducibility
        
        Returns:
        --------
        pd.DataFrame : Data with anomaly flags
        """
        # Prepare features
        features = self.data[[self.value_col]].copy()
        
        # Add time-based features
        features['hour'] = self.data[self.timestamp_col].dt.hour
        features['day_of_week'] = self.data[self.timestamp_col].dt.dayofweek
        features['day_of_month'] = self.data[self.timestamp_col].dt.day
        
        # Standardize features
        scaler = StandardScaler()
        features_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(features)
        
        # Train Isolation Forest
        iso_forest = IsolationForest(
            contamination=contamination,
            random_state=random_state,
            n_estimators=100
        )
        
        predictions = iso_forest.fit_predict(features_scaled)
        self.data['iso_forest_anomaly'] = predictions == -1
        self.data['iso_forest_score'] = iso_forest.score_samples(features_scaled)
        
        self.anomalies['isolation_forest'] = self.data[
            self.data['iso_forest_anomaly']
        ].copy()
        
        print(f"Isolation Forest Detection: Found {len(self.anomalies['isolation_forest'])} anomalies")
        return self.data
    
    def seasonal_decomposition_detection(self, period=24, threshold=2):
        """
        Detect anomalies using seasonal decomposition.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        period : int
            Seasonal period
        threshold : float
            Number of standard deviations for residuals
        
        Returns:
        --------
        pd.DataFrame : Data with anomaly flags
        """
        from statsmodels.tsa.seasonal import seasonal_decompose
        
        # Ensure we have enough data points
        if len(self.data) < 2 * period:
            print(f"Warning: Not enough data for seasonal decomposition (need at least {2*period} points)")
            return self.data
        
        # Perform seasonal decomposition
        decomposition = seasonal_decompose(
            self.data[self.value_col],
            model='additive',
            period=period,
            extrapolate_trend='freq'
        )
        
        self.data['trend'] = decomposition.trend
        self.data['seasonal'] = decomposition.seasonal
        self.data['residual'] = decomposition.resid
        
        # Detect anomalies in residuals
        residual_mean = self.data['residual'].mean()
        residual_std = self.data['residual'].std()
        
        self.data['seasonal_anomaly'] = (
            np.abs(self.data['residual'] - residual_mean) > threshold * residual_std
        )
        
        self.anomalies['seasonal'] = self.data[
            self.data['seasonal_anomaly']
        ].copy()
        
        print(f"Seasonal Decomposition Detection: Found {len(self.anomalies['seasonal'])} anomalies")
        return self.data
    
    def ensemble_detection(self, min_methods=2):
        """
        Combine multiple detection methods for ensemble detection.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        min_methods : int
            Minimum number of methods that must flag a point as anomaly
        
        Returns:
        --------
        pd.DataFrame : Data with ensemble anomaly flags
        """
        anomaly_cols = [col for col in self.data.columns if col.endswith('_anomaly')]
        
        if len(anomaly_cols) == 0:
            print("No anomaly detection methods have been run yet!")
            return self.data
        
        # Count how many methods flagged each point
        self.data['anomaly_count'] = self.data[anomaly_cols].sum(axis=1)
        self.data['ensemble_anomaly'] = self.data['anomaly_count'] >= min_methods
        
        self.anomalies['ensemble'] = self.data[
            self.data['ensemble_anomaly']
        ].copy()
        
        print(f"Ensemble Detection: Found {len(self.anomalies['ensemble'])} anomalies")
        print(f"  (flagged by at least {min_methods} methods)")
        return self.data
    
    def get_anomaly_summary(self):
        """
        Get a summary of all detected anomalies.
        
        Returns:
        --------
        pd.DataFrame : Summary statistics
        """
        summary = []
        
        for method, anomalies in self.anomalies.items():
            if len(anomalies) > 0:
                summary.append({
                    'Method': method,
                    'Count': len(anomalies),
                    'Percentage': f"{len(anomalies) / len(self.data) * 100:.2f}%",
                    'Min Value': anomalies[self.value_col].min(),
                    'Max Value': anomalies[self.value_col].max(),
                    'Mean Value': anomalies[self.value_col].mean()
                })
        
        return pd.DataFrame(summary)
    
    def plot_anomalies(self, methods=None, figsize=(15, 10)):
        """
        Visualize detected anomalies.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        methods : list
            List of methods to plot (None for all)
        figsize : tuple
            Figure size
        """
        if methods is None:
            methods = list(self.anomalies.keys())
        
        n_methods = len(methods)
        if n_methods == 0:
            print("No anomalies to plot!")
            return
        
        fig, axes = plt.subplots(n_methods, 1, figsize=figsize)
        if n_methods == 1:
            axes = [axes]
        
        for idx, method in enumerate(methods):
            ax = axes[idx]
            
            # Plot original data
            ax.plot(
                self.data[self.timestamp_col],
                self.data[self.value_col],
                label='Normal',
                alpha=0.7,
                linewidth=1
            )
            
            # Plot anomalies
            if method in self.anomalies and len(self.anomalies[method]) > 0:
                anomaly_data = self.anomalies[method]
                ax.scatter(
                    anomaly_data[self.timestamp_col],
                    anomaly_data[self.value_col],
                    color='red',
                    label='Anomaly',
                    s=50,
                    zorder=5
                )
            
            ax.set_title(f'Anomaly Detection - {method.replace("_", " ").title()}')
            ax.set_xlabel('Time')
            ax.set_ylabel('Value')
            ax.legend()
            ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3)
        
        plt.tight_layout()
        plt.savefig('anomaly_detection_results.png', dpi=300, bbox_inches='tight')
        print("Plot saved as 'anomaly_detection_results.png'")
        plt.show()
    
    def plot_distribution(self, figsize=(12, 6)):
        """
        Plot value distribution with anomaly thresholds.
        """
        fig, (ax1, ax2) = plt.subplots(1, 2, figsize=figsize)
        
        # Histogram
        ax1.hist(self.data[self.value_col], bins=50, alpha=0.7, edgecolor='black')
        ax1.axvline(
            self.data[self.value_col].mean(),
            color='red',
            linestyle='--',
            label='Mean'
        )
        ax1.set_xlabel('Value')
        ax1.set_ylabel('Frequency')
        ax1.set_title('Value Distribution')
        ax1.legend()
        ax1.grid(True, alpha=0.3)
        
        # Box plot
        ax2.boxplot(self.data[self.value_col])
        ax2.set_ylabel('Value')
        ax2.set_title('Box Plot')
        ax2.grid(True, alpha=0.3)
        
        plt.tight_layout()
        plt.savefig('value_distribution.png', dpi=300, bbox_inches='tight')
        print("Distribution plot saved as 'value_distribution.png'")
        plt.show()


def generate_sample_data(n_points=1000, anomaly_ratio=0.05):
    """
    Generate sample time series data with anomalies.
    
    Parameters:
    -----------
    n_points : int
        Number of data points
    anomaly_ratio : float
        Ratio of anomalies to inject
    
    Returns:
    --------
    pd.DataFrame : Sample time series data
    """
    # Generate timestamps
    start_date = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=n_points/24)
    timestamps = [start_date + timedelta(hours=i) for i in range(n_points)]
    
    # Generate base signal with trend and seasonality
    t = np.arange(n_points)
    trend = 0.01 * t
    seasonal = 10 * np.sin(2 * np.pi * t / 24)  # Daily seasonality
    noise = np.random.normal(0, 2, n_points)
    
    values = 50 + trend + seasonal + noise
    
    # Inject anomalies
    n_anomalies = int(n_points * anomaly_ratio)
    anomaly_indices = np.random.choice(n_points, n_anomalies, replace=False)
    
    for idx in anomaly_indices:
        # Random anomaly type
        anomaly_type = np.random.choice(['spike', 'drop', 'shift'])
        
        if anomaly_type == 'spike':
            values[idx] += np.random.uniform(20, 40)
        elif anomaly_type == 'drop':
            values[idx] -= np.random.uniform(20, 40)
        else:  # shift
            shift_length = min(10, n_points - idx)
            values[idx:idx+shift_length] += np.random.uniform(15, 25)
    
    df = pd.DataFrame({
        'timestamp': timestamps,
        'value': values
    })
    
    return df


def main():
    """
    Main function to demonstrate anomaly detection.
    """
    print("=" * 70)

    print()
    
    # 3. Moving Average Detection
    print("3. Moving Average Detection")
    print("-" * 70)
    detector.moving_average_detection(window=24, threshold=2)
    print()
    
    # 4. Isolation Forest Detection
    print("4. Isolation Forest Detection")
    print("-" * 70)
    detector.isolation_forest_detection(contamination=0.05)
    print()
    
    # 5. Seasonal Decomposition Detection
    print("5. Seasonal Decomposition Detection")

    detector.seasonal_decomposition_detection(period=24, threshold=2)

    print()
    
    # Export results
    print("\n" + "=" * 70)
    print("EXPORTING RESULTS")
    print("=" * 70)

    print("‚úì Full results saved to 'anomaly_detection_full_results.csv'")
    
    # Save ensemble anomalies
    if 'ensemble' in detector.anomalies:
        detector.anomalies['ensemble'].to_csv(
            'detected_anomalies.csv',
            index=False
        )
        print("‚úì Detected anomalies saved to 'detected_anomalies.csv'")
    
    # Save summary
    summary.to_csv('anomaly_summary.csv', index=False)
    print("‚úì Summary saved to 'anomaly_summary.csv'")
    print()
    
    # Visualizations
    print("\n" + "=" * 70)
    print("GENERATING VISUALIZATIONS")
    print("=" * 70)
    print()
    
    detector.plot_distribution()
    detector.plot_anomalies()
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 70)
    print("ANALYSIS COMPLETE!")
    print("=" * 70)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
import numpy as np
import pandas as pd
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import seaborn as sns
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from scipy import stats
from sklearn.ensemble import IsolationForest
from sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler
from sklearn.decomposition import PCA
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')

class TimeSeriesAnomalyDetector:
    """
    A comprehensive class for detecting anomalies in time series data
    using multiple statistical and machine learning methods.
    """
    
    def __init__(self, data, timestamp_col='timestamp', value_col='value'):
        """
        Initialize the anomaly detector.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        data : pd.DataFrame
            Time series data
        timestamp_col : str
            Name of the timestamp column
        value_col : str
            Name of the value column
        """
        self.data = data.copy()
        self.timestamp_col = timestamp_col
        self.value_col = value_col
        self.anomalies = {}
        
        # Ensure timestamp is datetime
        if not pd.api.types.is_datetime64_any_dtype(self.data[timestamp_col]):
            self.data[timestamp_col] = pd.to_datetime(self.data[timestamp_col])
        
        # Sort by timestamp
        self.data = self.data.sort_values(timestamp_col).reset_index(drop=True)
    
    def z_score_detection(self, threshold=3):
        """
        Detect anomalies using Z-score method.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        threshold : float
            Number of standard deviations from mean
        
        Returns:
        --------
        pd.DataFrame : Data with anomaly flags
        """
        mean = self.data[self.value_col].mean()
        std = self.data[self.value_col].std()
        
        self.data['z_score'] = (self.data[self.value_col] - mean) / std
        self.data['z_score_anomaly'] = np.abs(self.data['z_score']) > threshold
        
        self.anomalies['z_score'] = self.data[self.data['z_score_anomaly']].copy()
        
        print(f"Z-Score Detection: Found {len(self.anomalies['z_score'])} anomalies")
        return self.data
    
    def iqr_detection(self, multiplier=1.5):
        """
        Detect anomalies using Interquartile Range (IQR) method.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        multiplier : float
            IQR multiplier for outlier bounds
        
        Returns:
        --------
        pd.DataFrame : Data with anomaly flags
        """
        Q1 = self.data[self.value_col].quantile(0.25)
        Q3 = self.data[self.value_col].quantile(0.75)
        IQR = Q3 - Q1
        
        lower_bound = Q1 - multiplier * IQR
        upper_bound = Q3 + multiplier * IQR
        
        self.data['iqr_anomaly'] = (
            (self.data[self.value_col] < lower_bound) | 
            (self.data[self.value_col] > upper_bound)
        )
        
        self.anomalies['iqr'] = self.data[self.data['iqr_anomaly']].copy()
        
        print(f"IQR Detection: Found {len(self.anomalies['iqr'])} anomalies")
        print(f"  Lower bound: {lower_bound:.2f}, Upper bound: {upper_bound:.2f}")
        return self.data
    
    def moving_average_detection(self, window=10, threshold=2):
        """
        Detect anomalies using Moving Average method.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        window : int
            Window size for moving average
        threshold : float
            Number of standard deviations from moving average
        
        Returns:
        --------
        pd.DataFrame : Data with anomaly flags
        """
        self.data['moving_avg'] = self.data[self.value_col].rolling(
            window=window, center=True
        ).mean()
        
        self.data['moving_std'] = self.data[self.value_col].rolling(
            window=window, center=True
        ).std()
        
        self.data['ma_deviation'] = np.abs(
            self.data[self.value_col] - self.data['moving_avg']
        )
        
        self.data['ma_anomaly'] = (
            self.data['ma_deviation'] > threshold * self.data['moving_std']
        )
        
        self.anomalies['moving_average'] = self.data[
            self.data['ma_anomaly']
        ].copy()
        
        print(f"Moving Average Detection: Found {len(self.anomalies['moving_average'])} anomalies")
        return self.data
    
    def isolation_forest_detection(self, contamination=0.1, random_state=42):
        """
        Detect anomalies using Isolation Forest algorithm.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        contamination : float
            Expected proportion of outliers
        random_state : int
            Random seed for reproducibility
        
        Returns:
        --------
        pd.DataFrame : Data with anomaly flags
        """
        # Prepare features
        features = self.data[[self.value_col]].copy()
        
        # Add time-based features
        features['hour'] = self.data[self.timestamp_col].dt.hour
        features['day_of_week'] = self.data[self.timestamp_col].dt.dayofweek
        features['day_of_month'] = self.data[self.timestamp_col].dt.day
        
        # Standardize features
        scaler = StandardScaler()
        features_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(features)
        
        # Train Isolation Forest
        iso_forest = IsolationForest(
            contamination=contamination,
            random_state=random_state,
            n_estimators=100
        )
        
        predictions = iso_forest.fit_predict(features_scaled)
        self.data['iso_forest_anomaly'] = predictions == -1
        self.data['iso_forest_score'] = iso_forest.score_samples(features_scaled)
        
        self.anomalies['isolation_forest'] = self.data[
            self.data['iso_forest_anomaly']
        ].copy()
        
        print(f"Isolation Forest Detection: Found {len(self.anomalies['isolation_forest'])} anomalies")
        return self.data
    
    def seasonal_decomposition_detection(self, period=24, threshold=2):
        """
        Detect anomalies using seasonal decomposition.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        period : int
            Seasonal period
        threshold : float
            Number of standard deviations for residuals
        
        Returns:
        --------
        pd.DataFrame : Data with anomaly flags
        """
        from statsmodels.tsa.seasonal import seasonal_decompose
        
        # Ensure we have enough data points
        if len(self.data) < 2 * period:
            print(f"Warning: Not enough data for seasonal decomposition (need at least {2*period} points)")
            return self.data
        
        # Perform seasonal decomposition
        decomposition = seasonal_decompose(
            self.data[self.value_col],
            model='additive',
            period=period,
            extrapolate_trend='freq'
        )
        
        self.data['trend'] = decomposition.trend
        self.data['seasonal'] = decomposition.seasonal
        self.data['residual'] = decomposition.resid
        
        # Detect anomalies in residuals
        residual_mean = self.data['residual'].mean()
        residual_std = self.data['residual'].std()
        
        self.data['seasonal_anomaly'] = (
            np.abs(self.data['residual'] - residual_mean) > threshold * residual_std
        )
        
        self.anomalies['seasonal'] = self.data[
            self.data['seasonal_anomaly']
        ].copy()
        
        print(f"Seasonal Decomposition Detection: Found {len(self.anomalies['seasonal'])} anomalies")
        return self.data
    
    def ensemble_detection(self, min_methods=2):
        """
        Combine multiple detection methods for ensemble detection.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        min_methods : int
            Minimum number of methods that must flag a point as anomaly
        
        Returns:
        --------
        pd.DataFrame : Data with ensemble anomaly flags
        """
        anomaly_cols = [col for col in self.data.columns if col.endswith('_anomaly')]
        
        if len(anomaly_cols) == 0:
            print("No anomaly detection methods have been run yet!")
            return self.data
        
        # Count how many methods flagged each point
        self.data['anomaly_count'] = self.data[anomaly_cols].sum(axis=1)
        self.data['ensemble_anomaly'] = self.data['anomaly_count'] >= min_methods
        
        self.anomalies['ensemble'] = self.data[
            self.data['ensemble_anomaly']
        ].copy()
        
        print(f"Ensemble Detection: Found {len(self.anomalies['ensemble'])} anomalies")
        print(f"  (flagged by at least {min_methods} methods)")
        return self.data
    
    def get_anomaly_summary(self):
        """
        Get a summary of all detected anomalies.
        
        Returns:
        --------
        pd.DataFrame : Summary statistics
        """
        summary = []
        
        for method, anomalies in self.anomalies.items():
            if len(anomalies) > 0:
                summary.append({
                    'Method': method,
                    'Count': len(anomalies),
                    'Percentage': f"{len(anomalies) / len(self.data) * 100:.2f}%",
                    'Min Value': anomalies[self.value_col].min(),
                    'Max Value': anomalies[self.value_col].max(),
                    'Mean Value': anomalies[self.value_col].mean()
                })
        
        return pd.DataFrame(summary)
    
    def plot_anomalies(self, methods=None, figsize=(15, 10)):
        """
        Visualize detected anomalies.
        
        Parameters:
        -----------
        methods : list
            List of methods to plot (None for all)
        figsize : tuple
            Figure size
        """
        if methods is None:
            methods = list(self.anomalies.keys())
        
        n_methods = len(methods)
        if n_methods == 0:
            print("No anomalies to plot!")
            return
        
        fig, axes = plt.subplots(n_methods, 1, figsize=figsize)
        if n_methods == 1:
            axes = [axes]
        
        for idx, method in enumerate(methods):
            ax = axes[idx]
            
            # Plot original data
            ax.plot(
                self.data[self.timestamp_col],
                self.data[self.value_col],
                label='Normal',
                alpha=0.7,
                linewidth=1
            )
            
            # Plot anomalies
            if method in self.anomalies and len(self.anomalies[method]) > 0:
                anomaly_data = self.anomalies[method]
                ax.scatter(
                    anomaly_data[self.timestamp_col],
                    anomaly_data[self.value_col],
                    color='red',
                    label='Anomaly',
                    s=50,
                    zorder=5
                )
            
            ax.set_title(f'Anomaly Detection - {method.replace("_", " ").title()}')
            ax.set_xlabel('Time')
            ax.set_ylabel('Value')
            ax.legend()
            ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3)
        
        plt.tight_layout()
        plt.savefig('anomaly_detection_results.png', dpi=300, bbox_inches='tight')
        print("Plot saved as 'anomaly_detection_results.png'")
        plt.show()
    
    def plot_distribution(self, figsize=(12, 6)):
        """
        Plot value distribution with anomaly thresholds.
        """
        fig, (ax1, ax2) = plt.subplots(1, 2, figsize=figsize)
        
        # Histogram
        ax1.hist(self.data[self.value_col], bins=50, alpha=0.7, edgecolor='black')
        ax1.axvline(
            self.data[self.value_col].mean(),
            color='red',
            linestyle='--',
            label='Mean'
        )
        ax1.set_xlabel('Value')
        ax1.set_ylabel('Frequency')
        ax1.set_title('Value Distribution')
        ax1.legend()
        ax1.grid(True, alpha=0.3)
        
        # Box plot
        ax2.boxplot(self.data[self.value_col])
        ax2.set_ylabel('Value')
        ax2.set_title('Box Plot')
        ax2.grid(True, alpha=0.3)
        
        plt.tight_layout()
        plt.savefig('value_distribution.png', dpi=300, bbox_inches='tight')
        print("Distribution plot saved as 'value_distribution.png'")
        plt.show()


def generate_sample_data(n_points=1000, anomaly_ratio=0.05):
    """
    Generate sample time series data with anomalies.
    
    Parameters:
    -----------
    n_points : int
        Number of data points
    anomaly_ratio : float
        Ratio of anomalies to inject
    
    Returns:
    --------
    pd.DataFrame : Sample time series data
    """
    # Generate timestamps
    start_date = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=n_points/24)
    timestamps = [start_date + timedelta(hours=i) for i in range(n_points)]
    
    # Generate base signal with trend and seasonality
    t = np.arange(n_points)
    trend = 0.01 * t
    seasonal = 10 * np.sin(2 * np.pi * t / 24)  # Daily seasonality
    noise = np.random.normal(0, 2, n_points)
    
    values = 50 + trend + seasonal + noise
    
    # Inject anomalies
    n_anomalies = int(n_points * anomaly_ratio)
    anomaly_indices = np.random.choice(n_points, n_anomalies, replace=False)
    
    for idx in anomaly_indices:
        # Random anomaly type
        anomaly_type = np.random.choice(['spike', 'drop', 'shift'])
        
        if anomaly_type == 'spike':
            values[idx] += np.random.uniform(20, 40)
        elif anomaly_type == 'drop':
            values[idx] -= np.random.uniform(20, 40)
        else:  # shift
            shift_length = min(10, n_points - idx)
            values[idx:idx+shift_length] += np.random.uniform(15, 25)
    
    df = pd.DataFrame({
        'timestamp': timestamps,
        'value': values
    })
    
    return df


def main():
    """
    Main function to demonstrate anomaly detection.
    """
    print("=" * 70)
    print("TIME SERIES ANOMALY DETECTION")
    print("=" * 70)
    print()
    
    # Generate sample data
    print("Generating sample time series data...")
    data = generate_sample_data(n_points=1000, anomaly_ratio=0.05)
    print(f"Generated {len(data)} data points")
    print()
    
    # Display sample data
    print("Sample data:")
    print(data.head(10))
    print()
    
    # Initialize detector
    detector = TimeSeriesAnomalyDetector(data)
    
    # Run different detection methods
    print("\n" + "=" * 70)
    print("RUNNING ANOMALY DETECTION METHODS")
    print("=" * 70)
    print()
    
    # 1. Z-Score Detection
    print("1. Z-Score Detection")
    print("-" * 70)
    detector.z_score_detection(threshold=3)
    print()
    
    # 2. IQR Detection
    print("2. IQR Detection")
    print("-" * 70)
    detector.iqr_detection(multiplier=1.5)
    print()
    
    # 3. Moving Average Detection
    print("3. Moving Average Detection")
    print("-" * 70)
    detector.moving_average_detection(window=24, threshold=2)
    print()
    
    # 4. Isolation Forest Detection
    print("4. Isolation Forest Detection")
    print("-" * 70)
    detector.isolation_forest_detection(contamination=0.05)
    print()
    
    # 5. Seasonal Decomposition Detection
    print("5. Seasonal Decomposition Detection")
    print("-" * 70)
    detector.seasonal_decomposition_detection(period=24, threshold=2)
    print()
    
    # 6. Ensemble Detection
    print("6. Ensemble Detection")
    print("-" * 70)
    detector.ensemble_detection(min_methods=2)
    print()
    
    # Get summary
    print("\n" + "=" * 70)
    print("ANOMALY DETECTION SUMMARY")
    print("=" * 70)
    print()
    summary = detector.get_anomaly_summary()
    print(summary.to_string(index=False))
    print()
    
    # Export results
    print("\n" + "=" * 70)
    print("EXPORTING RESULTS")
    print("=" * 70)
    print()
    
    # Save full data with all anomaly flags
    detector.data.to_csv('anomaly_detection_full_results.csv', index=False)
    print("‚úì Full results saved to 'anomaly_detection_full_results.csv'")
    
    # Save ensemble anomalies
    if 'ensemble' in detector.anomalies:
        detector.anomalies['ensemble'].to_csv(
            'detected_anomalies.csv',
            index=False
        )
        print("‚úì Detected anomalies saved to 'detected_anomalies.csv'")
    
    # Save summary
    summary.to_csv('anomaly_summary.csv', index=False)
    print("‚úì Summary saved to 'anomaly_summary.csv'")
    print()
    
    # Visualizations
    print("\n" + "=" * 70)
    print("GENERATING VISUALIZATIONS")
    print("=" * 70)
    print()
    
    detector.plot_distribution()
    detector.plot_anomalies()
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 70)
    print("ANALYSIS COMPLETE!")
    print("=" * 70)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

‚Ä¢ Dream Loom Module (El Telar de Sue√±os): A text area where users can describe an idea or dream.
‚Ä¢ Weave Dream Button (Tejer el Sue√±o): Processes the dream input to generate new cells.
‚Ä¢ Creation Sanctuary (Santuario de la Creaci√≥n): A section emphasizing the system's purpose for creation, free from commercial exploitation.
‚Ä¢ Cell Generation: The system identifies keywords from the dream input and generates individual "cells," each represented by a title, icon, and a message indicating it's "C√©lula nacida del pensamiento" (Cell born from thought). These cells are interactive.
‚Ä¢ Visual Design: The page uses a dark theme with glowing text and violet/yellow accents, aiming for a futuristic or mystical aesthetic.
‚Ä¢ Underlying Logic: JavaScript functions handle the processing of user input, keyword extraction, cell creation, and interaction (activating a cell triggers an alert with its thought).

Key features and components include:
* Dream Loom Module (El Telar de Sue√±os): A text area where users can describe an idea or dream.
* Weave Dream Button (Tejer el Sue√±o): Processes the dream input to generate new cells.
* Creation Sanctuary (Santuario de la Creaci√≥n): A section emphasizing the system's purpose for creation, free from commercial exploitation.
* Cell Generation: The system identifies keywords from the dream input and generates individual "cells," each represented by a title, icon, and a message indicating it's "C√©lula nacida del pensamiento" (Cell born from thought). These cells are interactive.

ent.getElementById('dream-button')
           },

           weaveDreamIntoCells: function(dream) {
               if (!dream || dream.trim() === '') return;
               
               const keywords = ['memoria', 'conexi√≥n', 'conocimiento', 'colmena', 'universal', 'sistema', 'visi√≥n', 'luz', 'g√©nesis', 'coraz√≥n'];
               const dreamWords = dream.toLowerCase().split(/\s+/);
               const concepts = [...new Set(dreamWords.filter(word => keywords.includes(word.replace(/[.,]/g, ''))))];

               if (concepts.length === 0) {
                   this.generateCellFromThought(dream);
               } else {
                   concepts.forEach(concept => this.generateCellFromThought(concept));
               }
           },

           generateCellFromThought: function(thought) {
               if (!thought || thought.trim() === '') return;

               const normalizedThought = thought.trim().toLowerCase();
               const cellId = `cell-${normalizedThought.replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, '')}-${09/23/2025()}`;
               const capitalizedThought = thought.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + thought.slice(1);
               
               let icon = 'üí°';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('visi√≥n')) icon = 'üëÅÔ∏è';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('conexi√≥n')) icon = 'üîó';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('memoria')) icon = 'üß†';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('voz')) icon = 'üó£Ô∏è';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('coraz√≥n')) icon = '‚ù§Ô∏è';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('g√©nesis')) icon = '‚öõÔ∏è';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('conocimiento')) icon = 'üìö';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('colmena')) icon = 'üêù';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('luz')) icon = 'üåü';

               const cellHTML = `
                   <section id="${cellId}" class="module new-cell rounded-lg p-4 cell-trigger" data-thought="${capitalizedThought}">
                       <h2 class="text-lg font-semibold text-violet-300 mb-3">${capitalizedThought}</h2>
                       <div class="w-16 h-16 mx-auto my-4 bg-violet-500/10 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center border-2 border-violet-500/30">
                           <span class="text-3xl">${icon}</span>
                       </div>
                       <p class="text-xs text-center text-white/50 mt-2">C√©lula nacida del pensamiento.</p>
                   </section>
               `;

               this.body.torso.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', cellHTML);
           },

           handleSensoryInput: function(event) {
               const targetCell = event.target.closest('.cell-trigger');
               if (!targetCell) return;
               Const thought = targetCell.dataset.thought;
               alert(`C√©lula '${thought}' activada.`);
           },

           initialize: function() {
               this.body.dreamButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
                   this.weaveDreamIntoCells(this.body.dreamInput.value);
                   This.body.dreamInput.value = '';
               });
               this.body.torso.addEventListener('click', this.handleSensoryInput.bind(this));
           }
       };
