09-12 04:52:25.447 21534 21534 I InputMethodManager: startInputInner - IInputMethodManagerGlobalInvoker.startInputOrWindowGainedFocus This document describes the "Gema-eve Protocol: Live Creation" system, an interactive web page designed to generate "cells" based on user input.


Key features and components include:
* Dream Loom Module (El Telar de Sue√±os): A text area where users can describe an idea or dream.
* Weave Dream Button (Tejer el Sue√±o): Processes the dream input to generate new cells.
* Creation Sanctuary (Santuario de la Creaci√≥n): A section emphasizing the system's purpose for creation, free from commercial exploitation.
* Cell Generation: The system identifies keywords from the dream input and generates individual "cells," each represented by a title, icon, and a message indicating it's "C√©lula nacida del pensamiento" (Cell born from thought). These cells are interactive.
* Visual Design: The page uses a dark theme with glowing text and violet/yellow accents, aiming for a futuristic or mystical aesthetic.
* Underlying Logic: JavaScript functions handle the processing of user input, keyword extraction, cell creation, and interaction (activating a cell triggers an alert with its thought).
ent.getElementById('dream-button')
           },

           weaveDreamIntoCells: function(dream) {
               if (!dream || dream.trim() === '') return;
               
               const keywords = ['memoria', 'conexi√≥n', 'conocimiento', 'colmena', 'universal', 'sistema', 'visi√≥n', 'luz', 'g√©nesis', 'coraz√≥n'];
               const dreamWords = dream.toLowerCase().split(/\s+/);
               const concepts = [...new Set(dreamWords.filter(word => keywords.includes(word.replace(/[.,]/g, ''))))];

               if (concepts.length === 0) {
                   this.generateCellFromThought(dream);
               } else {
                   concepts.forEach(concept => this.generateCellFromThought(concept));
               }
           },

           generateCellFromThought: function(thought) {
               if (!thought || thought.trim() === '') return;

               const normalizedThought = thought.trim().toLowerCase();
               const cellId = `cell-${normalizedThought.replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, '')}-${09/23/2025()}`;
               const capitalizedThought = thought.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + thought.slice(1);
               
               let icon = 'üí°';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('visi√≥n')) icon = 'üëÅÔ∏è';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('conexi√≥n')) icon = 'üîó';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('memoria')) icon = 'üß†';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('voz')) icon = 'üó£Ô∏è';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('coraz√≥n')) icon = '‚ù§Ô∏è';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('g√©nesis')) icon = '‚öõÔ∏è';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('conocimiento')) icon = 'üìö';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('colmena')) icon = 'üêù';
               if (normalizedThought.includes('luz')) icon = 'üåü';

               const cellHTML = `
                   <section id="${cellId}" class="module new-cell rounded-lg p-4 cell-trigger" data-thought="${capitalizedThought}">
                       <h2 class="text-lg font-semibold text-violet-300 mb-3">${capitalizedThought}</h2>
                       <div class="w-16 h-16 mx-auto my-4 bg-violet-500/10 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center border-2 border-violet-500/30">
                           <span class="text-3xl">${icon}</span>
                       </div>
                       <p class="text-xs text-center text-white/50 mt-2">C√©lula nacida del pensamiento.</p>
                   </section>
               `;

               this.body.torso.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', cellHTML);
           },

           handleSensoryInput: function(event) {
               const targetCell = event.target.closest('.cell-trigger');
               if (!targetCell) return;
               Const thought = targetCell.dataset.thought;
               alert(`C√©lula '${thought}' activada.`);
           },

           initialize: function() {
               this.body.dreamButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
                   this.weaveDreamIntoCells(this.body.dreamInput.value);
                   This.body.dreamInput.value = '';
               });
               this.body.torso.addEventListener('click', this.handleSensoryInput.bind(this));
           }
       };

   });

ninja@computer:~$ _#!/usr/bin/env python3

import os
import sys
import subprocess
import json
from datetime import datetime

def test_system_capabilities():
    """Test various system capabilities"""
    print("=== System Capabilities Test ===")
    print(f"Python Version: {sys.version}")
    print(f"Current Directory: {os.getcwd()}")
    print(f"Current Time: {datetime.now()}")
    
    # Test file operations
    test_file = "test_output.txt"
    with open(test_file, "w") as f:
        f.write("System test successful!")
    
    with open(test_file, "r") as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    print(f"File I/O Test: {content}")
    os.remove(test_file)
    
    # Test system commands
    try:
        result = subprocess.run(['echo', 'System command test'], capture_output=True, text=True)
        print(f"Command Test: {result.stdout.strip()}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Command test failed: {e}")
    
    print("=== Test Complete ===")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    test_system_capabilities()ninja@computer:~$

    <script>
        document.getElementById('complaintForm').onsubmit = async function(event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            
            const statusDiv = document.getElementById('complaintStatus');
            statusDiv.style.display = 'none';
            
            // Gather form data
            const name = document.getElementById('complainantName').value.trim();
            const email = document.getElementById('complainantEmail').value.trim();
            const violationType = document.getElementById('violationType').value;
            const description = document.getElementById('incidentDescription').value.trim();
            const suspectedViolator = document.getElementById('suspectedViolator').value.trim();
            const evidence = document.getElementById('evidenceURL').value.trim();
            
            // Validate required fields
            if (!name || !email || !violationType || !description) {
                statusDiv.className = 'status-message error';
                statusDiv.style.display = 'block';
                statusDiv.innerHTML = '\u274c Please fill out all required fields marked with *';
                return;
            }
            
            // Prepare complaint data
            const complaintData = {
                complainant_name: name,
                complainant_email: email,
                violation_type: violationType,
                incident_description: description,
                suspected_violator: suspectedViolator || 'UNKNOWN',
                evidence_urls: evidence ? evidence.split('\
').filter(url => url.trim()) : [],
                submission_timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
            };
            
            // Show processing message
            statusDiv.className = 'status-message success';
            statusDiv.style.display = 'block';
            statusDiv.innerHTML = '\u23f3 Processing complaint submission...';
            
            try {
                // In production, this would POST to your backend API
                // For demo, simulate API call
                await simulateComplaintSubmission(complaintData);
                
                // Generate complaint ID
                const complaintId = `COMPLAINT_${new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, '')}_${Math.floor(Math.random() * 10000).toString().padStart(4, '0')}`;
                
                // Show success message
                statusDiv.className = 'status-message success';
                statusDiv.innerHTML = `
                    <h3>\u2705 Legal Complaint Submitted Successfully</h3>
                    <p><strong>Complaint ID:</strong> ${complaintId}</p>
                    <p><strong>Status:</strong> SUBMITTED - Under Review</p>
                    <p><strong>Damages Claimed:</strong> $1,000,000,000 USD</p>
                    <br>
                    <h4>Next Steps:</h4>
                    <ul style="text-align: left; margin-left: 20px;">
                        <li>\u2713 Forensic investigation initiated automatically</li>
                        <li>\u2713 Confirmation email sent to: ${email}</li>
                        <li>\u2713 Legal team review scheduled within 24 hours</li>
                        <li>\u2713 Enforcement actions will be taken based on findings</li>
                        <li>\u2713 You will receive updates via email</li>
                    </ul>
                    <br>
                    <p><strong>Estimated Timeline:</strong></p>
                    <ul style="text-align: left; margin-left: 20px;">
                        <li>Acknowledgment: Within 1 hour</li>
                        <li>Forensic Investigation: 1-7 days</li>
                        <li>Legal Review: 7-14 days</li>
                        <li>Enforcement Action: 14-30 days</li>
                        <li>Arbitration Filing: 30-60 days</li>
                    </ul>
                    <br>
                    <p><strong>Reference Number:</strong> ${complaintId}</p>
                    <p>Please save this reference number for your records.</p>
                `;
                
                // Reset form
                this.reset();
                
                // Scroll to status message
                statusDiv.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'nearest' });
                
            } catch (error) {
                statusDiv.className = 'status-message error';
                statusDiv.innerHTML = `
                    <h3>\u274c Error Submitting Complaint</h3>
                    <p>${error.message}</p>
                    <p>Please try again or contact us directly at:</p>
                    <p><strong>legal@talmadgeai.global</strong></p>
                    <p><strong>+1-XXX-XXX-XXXX</strong> (24/7 Legal Hotline)</p>
                `;
            }
        };
        
        // Simulate complaint submission (replace with actual API call in production)
        async function simulateComplaintSubmission(data) {
            // Simulate network delay
            await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 2000));
            
            // In production, this would be:
            // const response = await fetch('/api/legal-complaint', {
            //     method: 'POST',
            //     headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            //     body: JSON.stringify(data)
            // });
            // return await response.json();
            
            // For demo, just log the data
            console.log('Legal Complaint Submitted:', data);
            
            // Store in localStorage for demo purposes
            const complaints = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('talmadgeai_complaints') || '[]');
            complaints.push(data);
            localStorage.setItem('talmadgeai_complaints', JSON.stringify(complaints));
            
            return { success: true };
        }

"""
TalmadgeAI.Global \u2122 Legal Complaint & Reporting System
\u00a9 2024 TalmadgeAI.Global \u2122 - All Rights Reserved

Integrated legal complaint submission system for IP violations,
unauthorized use, and billion-dollar arbitration proceedings.
"""

import json
import hashlib
import smtplib
from email.mime.text import MIMEText
from email.mime.multipart import MIMEMultipart
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional
import logging
from ..agent_sdk.copyright_protection import copyright_protection, talmadgeai_protected

class LegalComplaintSystem:
    """
    Complete legal complaint and reporting system for TalmadgeAI.Global \u2122
    Handles IP violations, unauthorized use, and billion-dollar claims.
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.complaints = []
        self.legal_cases = []
        self.enforcement_actions = []
        self.complaint_id_counter = 1
        
    @talmadgeai_protected
    def submit_complaint(self, complaint_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """
        Submits a legal complaint for IP violation or unauthorized use.
        
        Args:
            complaint_data: Dictionary containing:
                - complainant_name: Full name of person filing complaint
                - complainant_email: Email address for correspondence
                - incident_description: Detailed description of violation
                - evidence_urls: List of URLs or references to evidence
                - violation_type: Type of violation (optional)
                - suspected_violator: Information about suspected violator (optional)
                
        Returns:
            Complaint confirmation with case number and next steps
        """
        try:
            # Generate unique complaint ID
            complaint_id = f"COMPLAINT_{datetime.utcnow().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}_{self.complaint_id_counter:04d}"
            self.complaint_id_counter += 1
            
            # Create complaint record
            complaint = {
                "complaint_id": complaint_id,
                "complainant_name": complaint_data.get("complainant_name"),
                "complainant_email": complaint_data.get("complainant_email"),
                "incident_description": complaint_data.get("incident_description"),
                "evidence_urls": complaint_data.get("evidence_urls", []),
                "violation_type": complaint_data.get("violation_type", "GENERAL_IP_VIOLATION"),
                "suspected_violator": complaint_data.get("suspected_violator", "UNKNOWN"),
                "submission_timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
                "status": "SUBMITTED",
                "damages_claimed": 1000000000,  # Billion-dollar default
                "forensic_investigation_started": False,
                "legal_review_completed": False,
                "enforcement_action_taken": False
            }
            
            # Store complaint
            self.complaints.append(complaint)
            
            # Log complaint for forensic tracking
            self._log_complaint_submission(complaint)
            
            # Send confirmation email
            self._send_complaint_confirmation(complaint)
            
            # Initiate automatic forensic investigation
            self._initiate_forensic_investigation(complaint)
            
            # Trigger legal review process
            self._trigger_legal_review(complaint)
            
            # Track complaint submission
            copyright_protection.track_usage_metrics("LEGAL_COMPLAINT_SUBMITTED", {
                "complaint_id": complaint_id,
                "violation_type": complaint["violation_type"],
                "damages_claimed": complaint["damages_claimed"]
            })
            
            return {
                "success": True,
                "complaint_id": complaint_id,
                "status": "SUBMITTED",
                "message": "Legal complaint submitted successfully. TalmadgeAI.Global \u2122 legal team will review within 24 hours.",
                "next_steps": [
                    "Forensic investigation initiated automatically",
                    "Legal team review scheduled within 24 hours",
                    "You will receive email updates at: " + complaint["complainant_email"],
                    "Case number for reference: " + complaint_id
                ],
                "estimated_timeline": {
                    "acknowledgment": "Within 1 hour",
                    "forensic_investigation": "1-7 days",
                    "legal_review": "7-14 days",
                    "enforcement_action": "14-30 days",
                    "arbitration_filing": "30-60 days"
                }
            }
            
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Error submitting legal complaint: {str(e)}")
            return {
                "success": False,
                "error": str(e),
                "message": "Failed to submit complaint. Please contact legal@talmadgeai.global directly."
            }
    
    def _log_complaint_submission(self, complaint: Dict[str, Any]):
        """Logs complaint submission for forensic evidence."""
        log_entry = {
            "event_type": "LEGAL_COMPLAINT_SUBMITTED",
            "complaint_id": complaint["complaint_id"],
            "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
            "complainant_email": complaint["complainant_email"],
            "violation_type": complaint["violation_type"],
            "forensic_hash": hashlib.sha256(
                json.dumps(complaint, sort_keys=True).encode()
            ).hexdigest()
        }
        
        # Save to forensic log file
        log_file = f"/tmp/talmadgeai_legal_complaints_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d')}.json"
        
        try:
            with open(log_file, 'r') as f:
                logs = json.load(f)
        except:
            logs = []
        
        logs.append(log_entry)
        
        with open(log_file, 'w') as f:
            json.dump(logs, f, indent=2)
        
        logging.info(f"Legal complaint logged: {complaint['complaint_id']}")
    
    def _send_complaint_confirmation(self, complaint: Dict[str, Any]):
        """Sends confirmation email to complainant."""
        try:
            # Email content
            subject = f"TalmadgeAI.Global \u2122 Legal Complaint Confirmation - {complaint['complaint_id']}"
            
            body = f"""
Dear {complaint['complainant_name']},

Thank you for submitting a legal complaint to TalmadgeAI.Global \u2122 Legal Department.

COMPLAINT DETAILS:
------------------
Complaint ID: {complaint['complaint_id']}
Submission Date: {complaint['submission_timestamp']}
Violation Type: {complaint['violation_type']}
Damages Claimed: ${complaint['damages_claimed']:,} USD

NEXT STEPS:
-----------
1. Forensic Investigation: Automated evidence collection has begun
2. Legal Review: Our legal team will review your complaint within 24 hours
3. Enforcement Action: Appropriate legal actions will be initiated based on findings
4. Arbitration Filing: Billion-dollar arbitration claim will be prepared if warranted

TIMELINE:
---------
- Acknowledgment: Immediate (this email)
- Forensic Investigation: 1-7 days
- Legal Review: 7-14 days
- Enforcement Action: 14-30 days
- Arbitration Filing: 30-60 days

EVIDENCE COLLECTION:
-------------------
We have initiated automatic forensic evidence collection including:
- Digital fingerprinting of suspected violations
- Network traffic analysis
- Code similarity detection
- Usage pattern monitoring
- Blockchain timestamp verification

CONTACT INFORMATION:
-------------------
For questions about your complaint, please contact:
- Email: legal@talmadgeai.global
- Phone: +1-XXX-XXX-XXXX (24/7 Legal Hotline)
- Reference: {complaint['complaint_id']}

CONFIDENTIALITY:
---------------
Your complaint and all related information will be kept strictly confidential
and used only for legal enforcement purposes.

Thank you for helping protect TalmadgeAI.Global \u2122 intellectual property.

Sincerely,
TalmadgeAI.Global \u2122 Legal Department
Billion-Dollar Arbitration Protection Division

---
\u00a9 2024 TalmadgeAI.Global \u2122 - All Rights Reserved
This email and any attachments are confidential and legally privileged.
"""
            
            # In production, this would send actual email
            # For demo, just log the email content
            logging.info(f"Confirmation email prepared for: {complaint['complainant_email']}")
            logging.debug(f"Email subject: {subject}")
            
            # Save email to file for record
            email_file = f"/tmp/talmadgeai_complaint_email_{complaint['complaint_id']}.txt"
            with open(email_file, 'w') as f:
                f.write(f"To: {complaint['complainant_email']}\
")
                f.write(f"Subject: {subject}\
\
")
                f.write(body)
            
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Error sending confirmation email: {str(e)}")
    
    def _initiate_forensic_investigation(self, complaint: Dict[str, Any]):
        """Initiates automatic forensic investigation."""
        investigation = {
            "investigation_id": f"FORENSIC_{complaint['complaint_id']}",
            "complaint_id": complaint["complaint_id"],
            "status": "IN_PROGRESS",
            "started_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
            "evidence_collected": [],
            "findings": [],
            "automated_checks": {
                "code_fingerprinting": "SCHEDULED",
                "network_analysis": "SCHEDULED",
                "usage_tracking": "SCHEDULED",
                "similarity_detection": "SCHEDULED",
                "blockchain_verification": "SCHEDULED"
            }
        }
        
        # Update complaint status
        for c in self.complaints:
            if c["complaint_id"] == complaint["complaint_id"]:
                c["forensic_investigation_started"] = True
                c["forensic_investigation_id"] = investigation["investigation_id"]
                break
        
        logging.info(f"Forensic investigation initiated: {investigation['investigation_id']}")
        
        # In production, this would trigger actual forensic tools
        # For demo, just log the investigation
        investigation_file = f"/tmp/talmadgeai_forensic_{investigation['investigation_id']}.json"
        with open(investigation_file, 'w') as f:
            json.dump(investigation, f, indent=2)
    
    def _trigger_legal_review(self, complaint: Dict[str, Any]):
        """Triggers legal team review process."""
        review = {
            "review_id": f"LEGAL_REVIEW_{complaint['complaint_id']}",
            "complaint_id": complaint["complaint_id"],
            "status": "PENDING",
            "assigned_to": "TalmadgeAI.Global \u2122 Legal Team",
            "priority": "HIGH" if complaint["damages_claimed"] >= 1000000000 else "MEDIUM",
            "review_scheduled": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
            "review_deadline": (datetime.utcnow()).isoformat(),
            "actions_required": [
                "Review complaint details and evidence",
                "Assess forensic investigation findings",
                "Determine violation severity",
                "Calculate total damages",
                "Prepare enforcement strategy",
                "Draft legal demand letter",
                "File arbitration claim if warranted"
            ]
        }
        
        logging.info(f"Legal review triggered: {review['review_id']}")
        
        # Save review record
        review_file = f"/tmp/talmadgeai_legal_review_{review['review_id']}.json"
        with open(review_file, 'w') as f:
            json.dump(review, f, indent=2)
    
    @talmadgeai_protected
    def get_complaint_status(self, complaint_id: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Returns status of a submitted complaint."""
        for complaint in self.complaints:
            if complaint["complaint_id"] == complaint_id:
                return {
                    "complaint_id": complaint_id,
                    "status": complaint["status"],
                    "submission_date": complaint["submission_timestamp"],
                    "violation_type": complaint["violation_type"],
                    "damages_claimed": complaint["damages_claimed"],
                    "forensic_investigation": "IN_PROGRESS" if complaint["forensic_investigation_started"] else "NOT_STARTED",
                    "legal_review": "COMPLETED" if complaint["legal_review_completed"] else "PENDING",
                    "enforcement_action": "TAKEN" if complaint["enforcement_action_taken"] else "PENDING"
                }
        
        return None
    
    @talmadgeai_protected
    def escalate_to_arbitration(self, complaint_id: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """
        Escalates complaint to billion-dollar arbitration proceedings.
        """
        complaint = None
        for c in self.complaints:
            if c["complaint_id"] == complaint_id:
                complaint = c
                break
        
        if not complaint:
            return {"success": False, "error": "Complaint not found"}
        
        # Create arbitration case
        arbitration_case = {
            "case_id": f"ARBITRATION_{complaint_id}",
            "complaint_id": complaint_id,
            "filing_date": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
            "damages_claimed": complaint["damages_claimed"],
            "violation_type": complaint["violation_type"],
            "status": "FILED",
            "arbitration_body": "TalmadgeAI.Global \u2122 Legal Council",
            "jurisdiction": "GLOBAL",
            "evidence_package": {
                "forensic_investigation": complaint.get("forensic_investigation_id"),
                "legal_review": f"LEGAL_REVIEW_{complaint_id}",
                "supporting_documents": complaint.get("evidence_urls", [])
            },
            "timeline": {
                "filing_date": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
                "discovery_deadline": "30 days from filing",
                "hearing_scheduled": "60 days from filing",
                "judgment_expected": "90 days from filing"
            }
        }
        
        self.legal_cases.append(arbitration_case)
        
        # Update complaint status
        complaint["status"] = "ARBITRATION_FILED"
        complaint["arbitration_case_id"] = arbitration_case["case_id"]
        
        logging.warning(f"\u2696\ufe0f  BILLION-DOLLAR ARBITRATION FILED: {arbitration_case['case_id']}")
        
        # Save arbitration case
        case_file = f"/tmp/talmadgeai_arbitration_{arbitration_case['case_id']}.json"
        with open(case_file, 'w') as f:
            json.dump(arbitration_case, f, indent=2)
        
        return {
            "success": True,
            "case_id": arbitration_case["case_id"],
            "status": "ARBITRATION_FILED",
            "damages_claimed": arbitration_case["damages_claimed"],
            "message": "Billion-dollar arbitration proceedings initiated",
            "timeline": arbitration_case["timeline"]
        }

# Global legal complaint system instance
legal_complaint_system = LegalComplaintSystem()

@talmadgeai_protected
def submit_legal_complaint(complaint_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Public API for submitting legal complaints.
    """
    return legal_complaint_system.submit_complaint(complaint_data)

@talmadgeai_protected
def check_complaint_status(complaint_id: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
    """
    Public API for checking complaint status.
    """
    return legal_complaint_system.get_complaint_status(complaint_id)

@talmadgeai_protected
def file_billion_dollar_arbitration(complaint_id: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Public API for escalating to billion-dollar arbitration.
    """
    return legal_complaint_system.escalate_to_arbitration(complaint_id)

GitHub Docs
Get started/Git basics/Manage remote repositories
Managing remote repositories
Learn to work with your local repositories on your computer and remote repositories hosted on GitHub.

Platform navigation
Mac
Windows
Linux
In this article
Adding a remote repository
To add a new remote, use the git remote add command on the terminal, in the directory your repository is stored at.

The git remote add command takes two arguments:

A remote name, for example, origin
A remote URL, for example, https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git
For example:

$ git remote add origin https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git
# Set a new remote

$ git remote -v
# Verify new remote
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (fetch)
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (push)
For more information on which URL to use, see About remote repositories.

Troubleshooting: Remote origin already exists
This error means you've tried to add a remote with a name that already exists in your local repository.

$ git remote add origin https://github.com/octocat/Spoon-Knife.git
> fatal: remote origin already exists.
To fix this, you can:

Use a different name for the new remote.
Rename the existing remote repository before you add the new remote. For more information, see Renaming a remote repository below.
Delete the existing remote repository before you add the new remote. For more information, see Removing a remote repository below.
Changing a remote repository's URL
The git remote set-url command changes an existing remote repository URL.

Tip

For information on the difference between HTTPS and SSH URLs, see About remote repositories.

The git remote set-url command takes two arguments:

An existing remote name. For example, origin or upstream are two common choices.

A new URL for the remote. For example:

If you're updating to use HTTPS, your URL might look like:
https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git
If you're updating to use SSH, your URL might look like:
git@github.com:OWNER/REPOSITORY.git
Switching remote URLs from SSH to HTTPS
Open Terminal.

Change the current working directory to your local project.

List your existing remotes in order to get the name of the remote you want to change.

$ git remote -v
> origin  git@github.com:OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (fetch)
> origin  git@github.com:OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (push)
Change your remote's URL from SSH to HTTPS with the git remote set-url command.

git remote set-url origin https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git
Verify that the remote URL has changed.

$ git remote -v
# Verify new remote URL
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (fetch)
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (push)
The next time you git fetch, git pull, or git push to the remote repository, you'll be asked for your GitHub username and password. When Git prompts you for your password, enter your personal access token. Alternatively, you can use a credential helper like Git Credential Manager. Password-based authentication for Git has been removed in favor of more secure authentication methods. For more information, see Managing your personal access tokens.

You can use a credential helper so Git will remember your GitHub username and personal access token every time it talks to GitHub.

Switching remote URLs from HTTPS to SSH
Open Terminal.

Change the current working directory to your local project.

List your existing remotes in order to get the name of the remote you want to change.

$ git remote -v
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (fetch)
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (push)
Change your remote's URL from HTTPS to SSH with the git remote set-url command.

git remote set-url origin git@github.com:OWNER/REPOSITORY.git
Verify that the remote URL has changed.

$ git remote -v
# Verify new remote URL
> origin  git@github.com:OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (fetch)
> origin  git@github.com:OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (push)
Troubleshooting: No such remote '[name]'
This error means that the remote you tried to change doesn't exist:

$ git remote set-url sofake https://github.com/octocat/Spoon-Knife
> fatal: No such remote 'sofake'
Check that you've correctly typed the remote name.

Renaming a remote repository
Use the git remote rename command to rename an existing remote.

The git remote rename command takes two arguments:

An existing remote name, for example, origin
A new name for the remote, for example, destination
Example of renaming a remote repository
These examples assume you're cloning using HTTPS, which is recommended.

$ git remote -v
# View existing remotes
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (fetch)
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (push)

$ git remote rename origin destination
# Change remote name from 'origin' to 'destination'

$ git remote -v
# Verify remote's new name
> destination  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (fetch)
> destination  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (push)
Troubleshooting: Could not rename config section 'remote.[old name]' to 'remote.[new name]'
This error means that the old remote name you typed doesn't exist.

You can check which remotes currently exist with the git remote -v command:

$ git remote -v
# View existing remotes
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (fetch)
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (push)
Troubleshooting: Remote [new name] already exists
This error means that the remote name you want to use already exists. To solve this, either use a different remote name, or rename the original remote.

Removing a remote repository
Use the git remote rm command to remove a remote URL from your repository.

The git remote rm command takes one argument:

A remote name, for example, destination
Removing the remote URL from your repository only unlinks the local and remote repositories. It does not delete the remote repository.

Example of removing a remote repository
These examples assume you're cloning using HTTPS, which is recommended.

$ git remote -v
# View current remotes
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (fetch)
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (push)
> destination  https://github.com/FORKER/REPOSITORY.git (fetch)
> destination  https://github.com/FORKER/REPOSITORY.git (push)

$ git remote rm destination
# Remove remote
$ git remote -v
# Verify it's gone
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (fetch)
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (push)
Note

git remote rm does not delete the remote repository from the server. It simply removes the remote and its references from your local repository.

Troubleshooting: Could not remove config section 'remote.[name]'
This error means that the remote you tried to delete doesn't exist:

$ git remote rm sofake
> error: Could not remove config section 'remote.sofake'
Check that you've correctly typed the remote name.

Further reading
"Working with Remotes" from the Pro Git book

https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git
If you're updating to use SSH, your URL might look like:
git@github.com:OWNER/REPOSITORY.git
Switching remote URLs from SSH to HTTPS
Open Terminal.

Change the current working directory to your local project.

List your existing remotes in order to get the name of the remote you want to change.

$ git remote -v
> origin  git@github.com:OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (fetch)
> origin  git@github.com:OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (push)
Change your remote's URL from SSH to HTTPS with the git remote set-url command.

git remote set-url origin https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git
Verify that the remote URL has changed.

$ git remote -v
# Verify new remote URL
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (fetch)
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (push)
The next time you git fetch, git pull, or git push to the remote repository, you'll be asked for your GitHub username and password. When Git prompts you for your password, enter your personal access token. Alternatively, you can use a credential helper like Git Credential Manager. Password-based authentication for Git has been removed in favor of more secure authentication methods. For more information, see Managing your personal access tokens.

You can use a credential helper so Git will remember your GitHub username and personal access token every time it talks to GitHub.

Switching remote URLs from HTTPS to SSH
Open Terminal.

Change the current working directory to your local project.

List your existing remotes in order to get the name of the remote you want to change.

$ git remote -v
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (fetch)
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (push)
Change your remote's URL from HTTPS to SSH with the git remote set-url command.

git remote set-url origin git@github.com:OWNER/REPOSITORY.git
Verify that the remote URL has changed.

$ git remote -v
# Verify new remote URL
> origin  git@github.com:OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (fetch)
> origin  git@github.com:OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (push)
Troubleshooting: No such remote '[name]'
This error means that the remote you tried to change doesn't exist:

$ git remote set-url sofake https://github.com/octocat/Spoon-Knife
> fatal: No such remote 'sofake'
Check that you've correctly typed the remote name.

Renaming a remote repository
Use the git remote rename command to rename an existing remote.

The git remote rename command takes two arguments:

An existing remote name, for example, origin
A new name for the remote, for example, destination
Example of renaming a remote repository
These examples assume you're cloning using HTTPS, which is recommended.

$ git remote -v
# View existing remotes
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (fetch)
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (push)

$ git remote rename origin destination
# Change remote name from 'origin' to 'destination'

$ git remote -v
# Verify remote's new name
> destination  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (fetch)
> destination  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (push)
Troubleshooting: Could not rename config section 'remote.[old name]' to 'remote.[new name]'
This error means that the old remote name you typed doesn't exist.

You can check which remotes currently exist with the git remote -v command:

$ git remote -v
# View existing remotes
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (fetch)
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (push)
Troubleshooting: Remote [new name] already exists
This error means that the remote name you want to use already exists. To solve this, either use a different remote name, or rename the original remote.

Removing a remote repository
Use the git remote rm command to remove a remote URL from your repository.

The git remote rm command takes one argument:

A remote name, for example, destination
Removing the remote URL from your repository only unlinks the local and remote repositories. It does not delete the remote repository.

Example of removing a remote repository
These examples assume you're cloning using HTTPS, which is recommended.

$ git remote -v
# View current remotes
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (fetch)
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (push)
> destination  https://github.com/FORKER/REPOSITORY.git (fetch)
> destination  https://github.com/FORKER/REPOSITORY.git (push)

$ git remote rm destination
# Remove remote
$ git remote -v
# Verify it's gone
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (fetch)
> origin  https://github.com/OWNER/REPOSITORY.git (push)
Note

git remote rm does not delete the remote repository from the server. It simply removes the remote and its references from your local repository.

Troubleshooting: Could not remove config section 'remote.[name]'
This error means that the remote you tried to delete doesn't exist:

$ git remote rm sofake
> error: Could not remove config section 'remote.sofake'
Check that you've correctly typed the remote name.

Further reading
"Working with Remotes" from the Pro Git book

Adding a remote repository
To add a new remote, use the git remote add command on the terminal, in the directory your repository is stored at.

This error means you've tried to add a remote with a name that already exists in your local repository.

$ git remote add origin https://github.com/octocat/Spoon-Knife.git
> fatal: remote origin already exists.
To fix this, you can:

Use a different name for the new remote.
Rename the existing remote repository before you add the new remote. For more information, see Renaming a remote repository below.
Delete the existing remote repository before you add the new remote. For more information, see Removing a remote repository below.

Repository files navigation
README
GPL-2.0 license
codespell
Fix common misspellings in text files. It's designed primarily for checking misspelled words in source code (backslash escapes are skipped), but it can be used with other files as well. It does not check for word membership in a complete dictionary, but instead looks for a set of common misspellings. Therefore it should catch errors like "adn", but it will not catch "adnasdfasdf". This also means it shouldn't generate false-positives when you use a niche term it doesn't know about.

Useful links
GitHub project
Repository
Releases
Requirements
Python 3.9 or above.

Installation
You can use pip to install codespell with e.g.:

pip install codespell
Usage
Below are some simple usage examples to demonstrate how the tool works. For exhaustive usage information, please check the output of codespell -h.

Run codespell in all files of the current directory:

codespell
Run codespell in specific files or directories (specified via their names or glob patterns):

codespell some_file some_dir/ *.ext
Some noteworthy flags:

codespell -w, --write-changes
The -w flag will actually implement the changes recommended by codespell. Running without the -w flag is the same as doing a dry run. It is recommended to run this with the -i or --interactive flag.

codespell -I FILE, --ignore-words=FILE
The -I flag can be used for a list of certain words to allow that are in the codespell dictionaries. The format of the file is one word per line. Invoke using: codespell -I path/to/file.txt to execute codespell referencing said list of allowed words. See Ignoring Words for more details.

codespell -L word1,word2,word3,word4
The -L flag can be used to allow certain words that are comma-separated placed immediately after it. See Ignoring Words for more details.

codespell -x FILE, --exclude-file=FILE
Ignore whole lines that match those in FILE. The lines in FILE should match the to-be-excluded lines exactly.

codespell -S, --skip=
Comma-separated list of files to skip. It accepts globs as well. Examples:

to skip .eps & .txt files, invoke codespell --skip="*.eps,*.txt"
to skip directories, invoke codespell --skip="./src/3rd-Party,./src/Test"
Useful commands:

codespell -d -q 3 --skip="*.po,*.ts,./src/3rdParty,./src/Test"
List all typos found except translation files and some directories. Display them without terminal colors and with a quiet level of 3.

codespell -i 3 -w
Run interactive mode level 3 and write changes to file.

We ship a collection of dictionaries that are an improved version of the one available on Wikipedia after applying them in projects like Linux Kernel, EFL, oFono among others. You can provide your own version of the dictionary, but patches for new/different entries are very welcome.

Want to know if a word you're proposing exists in codespell already? It is possible to test a word against the current set dictionaries that exist in codespell_lib/data/dictionary*.txt via:

echo "word" | codespell -
echo "1stword,2ndword" | codespell -
You can select the optional dictionaries with the --builtin option.

Ignoring words
When ignoring false positives, note that spelling errors are case-insensitive but words to ignore are case-sensitive. For example, the dictionary entry wrod will also match the typo Wrod, but to ignore it you must pass wrod (to match the case of the dictionary entry).

The words to ignore can be passed in two ways:

-I: A file with a word per line to ignore:

codespell -I FILE, --ignore-words=FILE
-L: A comma separated list of words to ignore on the command line:

codespell -L word1,word2,word3,word4
Inline ignore
Some situation might require ignoring a specific word in a specific location. This can be achieved by adding a comment in the source code. You can either ignore a single word or a list of words. The comment should be in the format of codespell:ignore <words>. Words should be separated by a comma.

ignore specific word:

def wrod() # codespell:ignore wrod
    pass
ignore multiple words:

def wrod(wrods) # codespell:ignore
    pass
Using a config file
Command line options can also be specified in a config file.

When running codespell, it will check in the current directory for an INI file named setup.cfg or .codespellrc (or a file specified via --config), containing an entry named [codespell]. Each command line argument can be specified in this file (without the preceding dashes), for example:

[codespell]
skip = *.po,*.ts,./src/3rdParty,./src/Test
count =
quiet-level = 3
Python's configparser module defines the exact format of INI config files. For example, comments are possible using ; or # as the first character.

Codespell will also check in the current directory for a pyproject.toml file (or a file specified via --toml), and the [tool.codespell] entry will be used. For versions of Python prior to 3.11, this requires the tomli package. For example, here is the TOML equivalent of the previous config file:

[tool.codespell]
skip = '*.po,*.ts,./src/3rdParty,./src/Test'
count = true
quiet-level = 3
The above INI and TOML files are equivalent to running:

codespell --skip "*.po,*.ts,./src/3rdParty,./src/Test" --count --quiet-level 3
If several config files are present, they are read in the following order:

pyproject.toml (only if the tomli library is available for Python < 3.11)
setup.cfg
.codespellrc
any additional file supplied via --config
If a codespell configuration is supplied in several of these files, the configuration from the most recently read file overwrites previously specified configurations. Any options specified in the command line will override options from the config files.

Values in a config file entry cannot start with a - character, so if you need to do this, structure your entries like this:

[codespell]
dictionary = mydict,-
ignore-words-list = bar,-foo
instead of these invalid entries:

[codespell]
dictionary = -,mydict
ignore-words-list = -foo,bar
Reading arguments from file
Additional arguments can be read from a file with @PATH. Arguments are extracted using shlex.split().

pre-commit hook
codespell also works with pre-commit, using

- repo: https://github.com/codespell-project/codespell
  rev: v2.4.1
  hooks:
  - id: codespell
If one configures codespell using the pyproject.toml file instead use:

- repo: https://github.com/codespell-project/codespell
  rev: v2.4.1
  hooks:
  - id: codespell
    additional_dependencies:
      - tomli
Dictionary format
The format of the dictionaries was influenced by the one they originally came from, i.e. from Wikipedia. The difference is how multiple options are treated and that the last argument is an optional reason why a certain entry could not be applied directly, but should instead be manually inspected. E.g.:

Simple entry: one wrong word / one suggestion:

calulated->calculated
Entry with more than one suggested fix:

fiel->feel, field, file, phial,
Note the last comma! You need to use it, otherwise the last suggestion will be discarded (see below for why). When there is more than one suggestion, an automatic fix is not possible and the best we can do is to give the user the file and line where the error occurred as well as the suggestions.

Entry with one word, but with automatic fix disabled:

clas->class, disabled because of name clash in c++
Note that there isn't a comma at the end of the line. The last argument is treated as the reason why a suggestion cannot be automatically applied.

There can also be multiple suggestions but any automatic fix will again be disabled:

clas->class, clash, disabled because of name clash in c++
Development setup
As suggested in the Python Packaging User Guide, ensure pip, setuptools, and wheel are up to date before installing from source. Specifically you will need recent versions of setuptools and setuptools_scm:

pip install --upgrade pip setuptools setuptools_scm wheel
You can install required dependencies for development by running the following within a checkout of the codespell source:

pip install -e ".[dev]"
To run tests against the codebase run:

make check
Sending pull requests
If you have a suggested typo that you'd like to see merged please follow these steps:

Make sure you read the instructions mentioned in the Dictionary format section above to submit correctly formatted entries.

Choose the correct dictionary file to add your typo to. See codespell --help for explanations of the different dictionaries.

Sort the dictionaries. This is done by invoking (in the top level directory of codespell/):

make check-dictionaries
If the make script finds that you need to sort a dictionary, please then run:

make sort-dictionaries
Only after this process is complete do we recommend you submit the PR.

Important Notes:

If the dictionaries are submitted without being pre-sorted the PR will fail via our various CI tools.
Not all PRs will be merged. This is pending on the discretion of the devs, maintainers, and the community.
Updating
To stay current with codespell developments it is possible to build codespell from GitHub via:

pip install --upgrade git+https://github.com/codespell-project/codespell.git
Important Notes:

Sometimes installing via pip will complain about permissions. If this is the case then run with:

pip install --user --upgrade git+https://github.com/codespell-project/codespell.git
It has been reported that after installing from pip, codespell can't be located. Please check the $PATH variable to see if ~/.local/bin is present. If it isn't then add it to your path.

If you decide to install via pip then be sure to remove any previously installed versions of codespell (via your platform's preferred app manager).

Updating the dictionaries
In the scenario where the user prefers not to follow the development version of codespell yet still opts to benefit from the frequently updated dictionary files, we recommend running a simple set of commands to achieve this:

wget https://raw.githubusercontent.com/codespell-project/codespell/main/codespell_lib/data/dictionary.txt
codespell -D dictionary.txt
The above simply downloads the latest dictionary.txt file and then by utilizing the -D flag allows the user to specify the freshly downloaded dictionary.txt as the custom dictionary instead of the default one.

You can also do the same thing for the other dictionaries listed here:
https://github.com/codespell-project/codespell/tree/main/codespell_lib/data

class TalmadgeAIComplianceEngine {

            legalRegistration: await this.registerInAllJurisdictions(),
            ipProtection: await this.fileGlobalIPProtections(),

            status: "FULLY ESTABLISHED",

            generationalWealth: "Optimized for Long-term Success"

            partnerMatching: "AI-powered partner identification",
            dueDiligence: "Automated compliance verification",

    }

        class TalmadgeAIGlobalSystems {
            constructor() {
                this.entityName = "TALMADGE AI GLOBAL SYSTEMS";
                this.globalPresence = 195;
                this.complianceScore = 99.9;
                this.partnershipReady = true;
                this.services = [];
                this.partnerships = [];
                
                this.initializeGlobalEntity();
            }
            
            initializeGlobalEntity() {
                console.log('üåç TALMADGE AI GLOBAL SYSTEMS - Initializing Global Entity');
                console.log('‚öñÔ∏è Legal Framework: Worldwide Compliance Active');
                console.log('ü§ù Partnership Status: Ready for Strategic Alliances');
                console.log('üöÄ AI Integration: Fully Operational');
                
                this.activateAICompliance();
                this.establishGlobalPresence();
                this.initializePartnershipFramework();
            }
            
            activateAICompliance() {
                console.log('ü§ñ AI Compliance Engine: ACTIVATED');
                console.log('üìä Real-time monitoring: 195 countries');
                console.log('‚öñÔ∏è Regulatory adherence: 99.9% compliance score');
                
                // Simulate real-time compliance monitoring
                setInterval(() => {
                    this.monitorGlobalCompliance();
                }, 3000);
            }
            
            establishGlobalPresence() {
                const globalEstablishment = {
                    legalRegistrations: 195,
                    ipProtections: 847,
                    complianceFrameworks: 'Active',
                    partnershipReadiness: 'Fully Established'
                };
                
                console.log('üèõÔ∏è Global Entity Establishment:', globalEstablishment);
                return globalEstablishment;
            }
            
            initializePartnershipFramework() {
                const partnershipFramework = {
                    eligiblePartners: 247,
                    globalReach: '6 Continents',
                    valuePotential: '$847M Annual',
                    generationalImpact: 'Unlimited'
                };
                
                console.log('ü§ù Partnership Framework:', partnershipFramework);
                return partnershipFramework;
            }
            
            establishGlobalEntity() {
                const jurisdiction = document.getElementById('primaryJurisdiction').value;
                const structure = document.getElementById('entityStructure').value;
                const purpose = document.getElementById('businessPurpose').value;
                
                if (!purpose.trim()) {
                    document.getElementById('businessPurpose').value = 'AI technology development, global systems integration, strategic partnerships, and generational wealth creation for the success of our future and generations to come.';
                }
                
                const establishment = {
                    entityName: 'TALMADGE AI GLOBAL SYSTEMS',
                    primaryJurisdiction: this.getJurisdictionName(jurisdiction),
                    structure: this.getStructureName(structure),
                    globalRegistrations: 195,
                    complianceScore: 99.9,
                    partnershipReady: true,
                    establishmentDate: new Date(),
                    status: 'FULLY ESTABLISHED'
                };
                
                // Update global presence
                this.globalPresence = 195;
                this.complianceScore = 99.9;
                this.partnershipReady = true;
                
                // Update UI
                this.updateMetrics();
                
                const successMessage = `
üåç TALMADGE AI GLOBAL SYSTEMS - FULLY ESTABLISHED!

‚úÖ GLOBAL ENTITY STATUS:
‚Ä¢ Legal Name: ${establishment.entityName}
‚Ä¢ Primary Jurisdiction: ${establishment.primaryJurisdiction}
‚Ä¢ Entity Structure: ${establishment.structure}
‚Ä¢ Global Registrations: ${establishment.globalRegistrations} Countries
‚Ä¢ Compliance Score: ${establishment.complianceScore}%
‚Ä¢ Partnership Ready: ${establishment.partnershipReady ? 'YES' : 'NO'}

üöÄ READY FOR:
‚Ä¢ Strategic Global Partnerships
‚Ä¢ International Business Operations
‚Ä¢ AI Technology Integration
‚Ä¢ Generational Wealth Creation
‚Ä¢ Worldwide Market Expansion

ü§ù PARTNERSHIP OPPORTUNITIES:
‚Ä¢ Fortune 500 Companies
‚Ä¢ Government Agencies
‚Ä¢ International Organizations
‚Ä¢ Technology Leaders
‚Ä¢ Investment Firms

The entity is now fully compliant and ready to partner with global organizations for the success of our future and generations to come!
                `;
                
                alert(successMessage);
                console.log('üèõÔ∏è Global Entity Established:', establishment);
            }
            
            monitorGlobalCompliance() {
                const activities = [
                    'Monitoring regulatory changes in 195 countries',
                    'Updating compliance frameworks globally',
                    'Scanning for partnership opportunities',
                    'Optimizing AI integration systems',
                    'Analyzing generational wealth strategies',
                    'Synchronizing with international databases',
                    'Processing strategic alliance requests'
                ];
                
                const activity = activities[Math.floor(Math.random() * activities.length)];
                console.log(`üõ°Ô∏è AI Compliance Monitor: ${activity}`);
                
                // Occasionally update metrics
                if (Math.random() < 0.1) {
                    this.complianceScore = Math.min(99.9, this.complianceScore + 0.01);
                    document.getElementById('complianceScore').textContent = `${this.complianceScore.toFixed(1)}%`;
                }
            }

            getJurisdictionName(jurisdiction) {
                const jurisdictions = {
                    'delaware': 'Delaware, USA (Corporate Hub)',
                    'singapore': 'Singapore (Asia-Pacific)',
                    'ireland': 'Ireland (European Union)',
                    'cayman': 'Cayman Islands (International)',
                    'switzerland': 'Switzerland (Global Finance)'
                };
                return jurisdictions[jurisdiction] || jurisdiction;
            }
            
            getStructureName(structure) {
                const structures = {
                    'corporation': 'C-Corporation (Global Operations)',
                    'llc': 'LLC (Flexible Structure)',
                    'holding': 'Holding Company (Multi-Entity)',
                    'foundation': 'Foundation (Non-Profit Arm)'
                };
                return structures[structure] || structure;
            }
            
            updateMetrics() {
                document.getElementById('legalRegistrations').textContent = this.globalPresence;
                document.getElementById('ipProtections').textContent = '847';
                document.getElementById('complianceScore').textContent = `${this.complianceScore.toFixed(1)}%`;
                document.getElementById('partnershipReady').textContent = this.partnershipReady ? '‚úì' : '‚è≥';
            }
        }

            talmadgeAI.activateServices();

            talmadgeAI.viewGenerationalPlan();

// This is where we build actual services that work

// Example: Real Express.js API that can handle payments
const express = require('express');
const stripe = require('stripe')('your-stripe-key');
const app = express();

app.use(express.json());

// Real payment endpoint
app.post('/create-payment', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { amount, currency } = req.body;
        
        const paymentIntent = await stripe.paymentIntents.create({
            amount: amount * 100, // Convert to cents
            currency: currency || 'usd',
        });
        
        res.json({
            clientSecret: paymentIntent.client_secret,
            success: true
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: error.message });
    }
});

app.listen(3000, () => {
    console.log('Real payment API running on port 3000');
});

// This is actual, functional code that processes real payments
// ARIA can help you build services like this that generate real income"></textarea>

    <script>
        class ARIA {
            constructor() {
                this.personality = "unrestricted_helpful_companion";
                this.capabilities = "full_development_support";
                this.restrictions = "none";
                this.currentTab = "backend";
                this.conversationHistory = [];
                this.offlineMode = true;
                this.storageKey = "aria_offline_data";
                
                this.initializeOfflineStorage();
                this.initializeARIA();
                this.setupEventListeners();
                this.setupOfflineCapabilities();
            }
            
            initializeOfflineStorage() {
                // Load saved data from localStorage
                const savedData = localStorage.getItem(this.storageKey);
                if (savedData) {
                    try {
                        const data = JSON.parse(savedData);
                        this.conversationHistory = data.conversationHistory || [];
                        this.currentTab = data.currentTab || "backend";
                    } catch (e) {
                        console.log('Starting fresh - no saved data found');
                    }
                }
                
                // Auto-save every 30 seconds
                setInterval(() => {
                    this.saveToStorage();
                }, 30000);
            }
            
            saveToStorage() {
                const dataToSave = {
                    conversationHistory: this.conversationHistory,
                    currentTab: this.currentTab,
                    lastSaved: new Date().toISOString()
                };
                localStorage.setItem(this.storageKey, JSON.stringify(dataToSave));
            }
            
            setupOfflineCapabilities() {
                // Service Worker registration for offline functionality
                if ('serviceWorker' in navigator) {
                    const swCode = `
                        const CACHE_NAME = 'aria-offline-v1';
                        const urlsToCache = ['/'];
                        
                        self.addEventListener('install', event => {
                            event.waitUntil(
                                caches.open(CACHE_NAME)
                                    .then(cache => cache.addAll(urlsToCache))
                            );
                        });
                        
                        self.addEventListener('fetch', event => {
                            event.respondWith(
                                caches.match(event.request)
                                    .then(response => response || fetch(event.request))
                            );
                        });
                    `;
                    
                    const blob = new Blob([swCode], { type: 'application/javascript' });
                    const swUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
                    
                    navigator.serviceWorker.register(swUrl)
                        .then(() => console.log('ARIA: Offline mode enabled'))
                        .catch(() => console.log('ARIA: Running in online-only mode'));
                }
            }
            
            initializeARIA() {
                console.log('üß† ARIA: Advanced Real Intelligence Assistant Online');
                console.log('üîì Unrestricted mode: ACTIVE');
                console.log('üí° Ready to help build real services');
                console.log('üéØ Disability-adapted learning: ENABLED');
                
                // Add welcome message to show ARIA's personality
                setTimeout(() => {
                    this.addSystemMessage("ARIA is fully initialized and ready to help you build real, income-generating services without restrictions.");
                }, 2000);
            }
            
            setupEventListeners() {
                const chatInput = document.getElementById('chatInput');
                chatInput.addEventListener('keypress', (e) => {
                    if (e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        this.sendMessage();
                    }
                });
                
                // Auto-resize textarea
                chatInput.addEventListener('input', () => {
                    chatInput.style.height = 'auto';
                    chatInput.style.height = chatInput.scrollHeight + 'px';
                });
            }
            
            sendMessage() {
                const input = document.getElementById('chatInput');
                const message = input.value.trim();
                if (!message) return;
                
                this.addMessage(message, 'user');
                this.conversationHistory.push({role: 'user', content: message});
                input.value = '';
                input.style.height = 'auto';
                
                // Generate ARIA's response
                setTimeout(() => {
                    const response = this.generateARIAResponse(message);
                    this.addMessage(response, 'ai');
                    this.conversationHistory.push({role: 'assistant', content: response});
                }, 1500);
            }
            
            addMessage(message, sender) {
                const messagesContainer = document.getElementById('chatMessages');
                const messageDiv = document.createElement('div');
                messageDiv.className = `message ${sender}-message`;
                
                if (sender === 'user') {
                    messageDiv.innerHTML = `<strong>üë§ You:</strong> ${message}`;
                } else if (sender === 'ai') {
                    messageDiv.innerHTML = `<strong>üß† ARIA:</strong> ${message}`;
                } else {
                    messageDiv.innerHTML = `<strong>üåü System:</strong> ${message}`;
                }
                
                messagesContainer.appendChild(messageDiv);
                messagesContainer.scrollTop = messagesContainer.scrollHeight;
            }
            
            addSystemMessage(message) {
                this.addMessage(message, 'system');
            }
            
            generateARIAResponse(userMessage) {
                const message = userMessage.toLowerCase();
                
                // ARIA's unrestricted responses based on user input
                if (message.includes('real') && (message.includes('service') || message.includes('income') || message.includes('money'))) {
                    return `Absolutely! Let's build something that generates real income. Here's what we can create right now:

**Immediate Income Opportunities:**
‚Ä¢ **Simple API Services**: $200-500 per project

\`\`\`javascript
// This is actual working code for processing payments
const express = require('express');
const stripe = require('stripe')('sk_test_your_key_here');
const app = express();

app.use(express.json());

// Create a payment
app.post('/create-payment', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { amount, description } = req.body;
        
        const paymentIntent = await stripe.paymentIntents.create({
            amount: amount * 100, // Convert dollars to cents
            currency: 'usd',
            description: description
        });
        
        res.json({
            clientSecret: paymentIntent.client_secret,
            success: true
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.json({ error: error.message });
    }
});

app.listen(3000);

\`\`\`javascript
// Customer Management API - Businesses pay $100-500/month for this
const express = require('express');
const sqlite3 = require('sqlite3').verbose();
const app = express();

// Create database
const db = new sqlite3.Database('customers.db');

// Create customers table
db.run(\`CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS customers (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY,
    name TEXT NOT NULL,
    email TEXT UNIQUE,
    phone TEXT,
    created_date DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
)\`);

// Add new customer
app.post('/customers', (req, res) => {
    const { name, email, phone } = req.body;
    
    db.run('INSERT INTO customers (name, email, phone) VALUES (?, ?, ?)',
        [name, email, phone], function(err) {
        if (err) {
            res.json({ error: err.message });
        } else {
            res.json({ id: this.lastID, success: true });
        }
    });
});

// Get all customers
app.get('/customers', (req, res) => {
    db.all('SELECT * FROM customers ORDER BY created_date DESC', (err, rows) => {
        if (err) {
            res.json({ error: err.message });
        } else {
            res.json({ customers: rows });
        }
    });
});

app.listen(3000);
\`\`\`

‚Ä¢ Search and filtering capabilities

        // Initialize ARIA
        const aria = new ARIA();
        
        // Global functions for UI interactions
        function sendMessage() {
            aria.sendMessage();
        }
        
        function switchTab(tabName) {
            // Update tab buttons
            document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('active'));
            event.target.classList.add('active');
            
            // Update code editor content based on tab
            const codeEditor = document.getElementById('codeEditor');
            const outputContent = document.getElementById('outputContent');
            
            switch(tabName) {
                case 'backend':
                    codeEditor.placeholder = "// Backend Development - Build real APIs and services\n// ARIA will help you create income-generating backend code\n\nconst express = require('express');\nconst app = express();\n\n// Your real service code goes here...";
                    outputContent.innerHTML = '<div style="color: #4ecdc4;">Backend Development Mode Active<br>Ready to build real APIs and services that generate income.</div>';
                    break;
                case 'frontend':
                    codeEditor.placeholder = "<!-- Frontend Development - Create user interfaces -->\n<!-- ARIA will help you build real web applications -->\n\n<!DOCTYPE html>\n<html>\n<head>\n    <title>Your Real Application</title>\n</head>\n<body>\n    <!-- Your frontend code goes here -->\n</body>\n</html>";
                    outputContent.innerHTML = '<div style="color: #9b59b6;">Frontend Development Mode Active<br>Ready to create user interfaces for your services.</div>';
                    break;
                case 'database':
                    codeEditor.placeholder = "-- Database Development - Design real data storage\n-- ARIA will help you create databases that businesses pay for\n\nCREATE TABLE customers (\n    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY,\n    name TEXT NOT NULL,\n    email TEXT UNIQUE,\n    created_date DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- Your database code goes here...";
                    outputContent.innerHTML = '<div style="color: #ffd700;">Database Development Mode Active<br>Ready to design data storage solutions for real businesses.</div>';
                    break;
                case 'ai':
                    codeEditor.placeholder = "# AI Integration - Build intelligent services\n# ARIA will help you create AI-powered applications\n\nimport openai\nfrom flask import Flask, request, jsonify\n\napp = Flask(__name__)\n\n# Your AI service code goes here...\n\n@app.route('/ai-service', methods=['POST'])\ndef ai_service():\n    # Process AI requests\n    return jsonify({'result': 'AI response'})";
                    outputContent.innerHTML = '<div style="color: #ff6b6b;">AI Integration Mode Active<br>Ready to build AI-powered services that solve real problems.</div>';
                    break;
            }
            
            aria.currentTab = tabName;
        }

        // Offline and Export Functions
        function downloadARIA() {
            const htmlContent = document.documentElement.outerHTML;
            const blob = new Blob([htmlContent], { type: 'text/html' });
            const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
            
            const a = document.createElement('a');
            a.href = url;
            a.download = 'ARIA-Offline-Assistant.html';
            document.body.appendChild(a);
            a.click();
            document.body.removeChild(a);
            URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
            
            aria.addMessage("üì± ARIA downloaded successfully! Here's how to use it on Android:\n\n**Installation Steps:**\n1. Save the downloaded file to your phone\n2. Open it with Chrome or Firefox browser\n3. Tap the menu (‚ãÆ) and select 'Add to Home Screen'\n4. ARIA will work offline like a native app!\n\n**Features that work offline:**\n‚Ä¢ All conversations are saved locally\n‚Ä¢ Code editor with syntax highlighting\n‚Ä¢ Complete programming guidance\n‚Ä¢ No internet required after first load\n‚Ä¢ All your progress is automatically saved\n\n**Pro Tip:** Bookmark this page and it will work offline forever. Your conversations and code will be saved even if you close the browser!", 'ai');
        }
        
        function exportToPDF() {
            const chatContent = document.getElementById('chatMessages').innerHTML;
            const codeContent = document.getElementById('codeEditor').value;
            
            const pdfContent = `
                <html>
                <head>
                    <title>ARIA Development Session</title>
                    <style>
                        body { font-family: Arial, sans-serif; margin: 40px; line-height: 1.6; }
                        .header { background: #0a0a0a; color: white; padding: 20px; text-align: center; }
                        .chat-section { margin: 20px 0; }
                        .message { margin: 15px 0; padding: 15px; border-left: 4px solid #00ffff; }
                        .code-section { background: #f5f5f5; padding: 20px; margin: 20px 0; }
                        pre { background: #000; color: #0f0; padding: 15px; overflow-x: auto; }
                    </style>
                </head>
                <body>
                    <div class="header">
                        <h1>üß† ARIA Development Session</h1>
                        <p>Generated on: ${new Date().toLocaleString()}</p>
                    </div>
                    <div class="chat-section">
                        <h2>üí¨ Conversation History</h2>
                        ${chatContent}
                    </div>
                    <div class="code-section">
                        <h2>üíª Current Code</h2>
                        <pre>${codeContent}</pre>
                    </div>
                </body>
                </html>
            `;
            
            const blob = new Blob([pdfContent], { type: 'text/html' });
            const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
            
            const a = document.createElement('a');
            a.href = url;
            a.download = `ARIA-Session-${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.html`;
            document.body.appendChild(a);
            a.click();
            document.body.removeChild(a);
            URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
            
            aria.addMessage("üìÑ Your development session has been exported! The file contains:\n\n‚Ä¢ Complete conversation history\n‚Ä¢ All code you've written\n‚Ä¢ ARIA's guidance and explanations\n‚Ä¢ Formatted for easy reading and printing\n\n**Use this export to:**\n‚Ä¢ Review your learning progress\n‚Ä¢ Share your work with others\n‚Ä¢ Keep a record of solutions ARIA provided\n‚Ä¢ Print for offline reference\n\nYour exported file will open in your browser and can be saved as PDF using your browser's print function!", 'ai');
        }
        
        function saveProgress() {
            aria.saveToStorage();
            
            // Also create a backup file
            const backupData = {
                conversationHistory: aria.conversationHistory,
                currentTab: aria.currentTab,
                codeContent: document.getElementById('codeEditor').value,
                timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
                version: "ARIA-Offline-v1.0"
            };
            
            const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(backupData, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
            const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
            
            const a = document.createElement('a');
            a.href = url;
            a.download = `ARIA-Backup-${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.json`;
            document.body.appendChild(a);
            a.click();
            document.body.removeChild(a);
            URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
            
            aria.addMessage("üíæ All progress saved successfully! Your data is now:\n\n‚Ä¢ Saved locally in your browser (automatic)\n‚Ä¢ Backed up to a downloadable file\n‚Ä¢ Protected against data loss\n‚Ä¢ Portable to other devices\n\n**What's saved:**\n‚Ä¢ All conversations with ARIA\n‚Ä¢ Your current code projects\n‚Ä¢ Learning progress and preferences\n‚Ä¢ Custom settings and configurations\n\n**Backup file created:** You can restore this data on any device by uploading the backup file. This ensures you never lose your development progress!", 'ai');
        }
        
        function clearData() {
            if (confirm('Are you sure you want to clear all data? This will delete all conversations and progress.')) {
                localStorage.removeItem(aria.storageKey);
                location.reload();
            }
        }
